# IdeaLoop Core — Narrative Contract Document V8-LOCKED + V9-OPEN (V11.30, June 22, 2026 — **THE EXPLORE-MODE RE-ENTRY QUESTION RESOLVED ("NO RE-EVAL MIRROR" — the divergence/measurement split), THE "FROM HERE" SECTION-4 REDESIGN (parent-scoped Save/Explore/Deep, the angle-steer KILLED), TAKE-TO HANDOFF ROUTING + AN UNSAVED-EXPLORATION LEAVE-GUARD, and THE EXPLORE QUALITY PASS — which REFINES the Explore output contract `ll2_explore_v1` (two NEW per-angle atoms `disconfirmer_kind` + `demand_evidenced` + CODE-DERIVED readiness/fan_state/branchability + a recalibrated route-owned density classification + a token-leak scrub) — plus the Explore RESULT-VIEW RE-WEIGHT** — ALL Explore-mode (engine-prompt / route / two route-side label-and-scrub passes + frontend), touching NO §3.x DEEP interpretation-surface CONTRACT, **NOT a V9.x amendment** (no §3.x DEEP surface, no Deep score formation, no `lookup[archetype][sub_position]`, no MB selection, no `overall_score`, no Deep scorer schema, no MO `display_score` / override-trace, no score-shape guard; the V5.0 DEEP scoring engine is BYTE-UNCHANGED in scoring terms at `bf09382` + the Arc-7→Arc-12 + LL1 + LL2 + V78 + V80 + V82 + V83 + V84 + V85 + V86 + V87 + V88 commits; **NO Supabase-SCHEMA change**). **WHY THIS TOUCHES NO V9 CONTRACT:** V9 governs the DEEP SCORING discipline; Explore is a SEPARATE mode with its OWN output contract (`ll2_explore_v1`), per V11.17/V11.18 — its surfaces are NOT §3.x DEEP surfaces. This session REFINES that Explore contract (it adds two per-angle atoms, moves the three honesty LABELS from model-self-report to code-derivation, recalibrates the route-owned density classification, and scrubs internal-id leaks from Explore prose) and re-weights the Explore renderer; none of it forms, re-encodes, or reports a DEEP score, and none of it adds or amends a §3 DEEP prose surface. **THE LOAD-BEARING DOCTRINE (recorded as the operative calls):** **(i) EXPLORE NEEDS NO RE-EVAL MIRROR — the divergence/measurement split (CONVERGENT across two independent Claude passes).** DeepEvolveView (V88) is a DELTA-MEASUREMENT instrument — the score is its spine; strip the score and nothing structural survives, and Explore already has the residue (`explore_variation` re-runs the fan, `edit_read` returns to input). The Explore prompt makes variance across runs EXPECTED AND CORRECT, so there is no stable baseline to diff — a "delta between two fans" is designed-in noise, not signal. Deep MEASURES; Explore WIDENS; re-eval-as-delta is DEEP's role in the loop and the boundary crossing (Take to Deep) is where measurement begins. The "Evolve mirror, NON-VERDICT" framing is RETIRED; renamed "Explore re-entry, divergence-shaped, no delta." **(ii) THE NON-RANKING LOCK HELD — the angle-steer killed (Emre's call).** Section 4 lists the options and gets out of the way; a surface pointing at one angle would break Explore's no-score / no-rank / no-verdict discipline. The recommendation paragraph / `nextMove.recommendation` ("take the PM angle to Deep") is REMOVED at both the button and the prose level; the OPEN QUESTION stays (the unresolved thing handed back is the opposite of advice). Section 4 acts on the WHOLE idea only (Save · Explore again · Take to Deep); per-angle decisions (save · explore · take to Deep) live under each angle card — same vocabulary at both scales, the parent control in one place, the angle controls in another. **(iii) CODE OWNS THE LABEL, MODEL OWNS THE ATOMS — the deflator architecture.** A model that stamps its own honesty grade always gives itself an A (fan_state rich 24/24, branchable 24/24, readiness worth_shaping 90%, the four planted thin edge-cases all rich). The cure: the synthesis EMITS two new per-angle atoms — `disconfirmer_kind` (5-value enum direct_incumbent_holds / free_substitute_floor / demand_unproven / structural_barrier / closeable_gap) + `demand_evidenced` (bool) — and the route DETERMINISTICALLY derives all three labels from them (readiness ← opening.trust × disconfirmer_kind × demand_evidenced; fan_state ← the readiness DISTRIBUTION; branchability ← reconciled), stashing originals as `_readiness_model` / `_state_model`. The model can't inflate a label it no longer holds the pen on — PHYSICAL SEPARATION again (the Stage 2a density re-derivation / the V9.30 MO `display_score` lever, applied to Explore's honesty labels); the route is the LABEL authority, the model the ATOM author. The honesty discipline was verified by the FOUNDER'S-EYE PROSE-READ (all 24/101 read twice): the deflation is HONEST not over-corrected (every thin idea thin because real strong current incumbents hold the lane), the residual was LENIENCY (cured by a one-line `demand_unproven → probably_thin ALWAYS` deriver fix, replay-verified, no re-run), and the disconfirmer prose was already doing the truth-telling the labels weren't. **WHAT THIS RECORDS (contract-relevant facts, since none is a DEEP-contract CHANGE):** **(1) `ll2_explore_v1` gains two per-angle atoms** — `disconfirmer_kind` (closed 5-value enum, strongest-deflator-wins, must AGREE with the kill sentence — "a kill naming a strong direct incumbent cannot be tagged closeable_gap") + `demand_evidenced` (bool). These are ATOMS the model commits, NOT self-reported labels; the route grades the labels off them. **(2) the three honesty labels are now CODE-DERIVED** — readiness / fan_state / branchability are computed by `applyDerivedLabels()` from the atoms (fan_state by the readiness distribution, NOT the old `angles.length` count), with the model's self-reports preserved as `_readiness_model` / `_state_model` for the probe; the frontend renders the EXISTING enums (incl. the previously-never-fired `partially_branchable`) — no new value invented, three labels kept. **(3) the route-owned DENSITY classification recalibrated** — `classifyDensityLane` was excluding famous-but-URL-less incumbents (`llm_generated`) from the "strong" count; split into `strongAny` (drives the count + ≥50% ratio) + `strongVerified` (a ≥1 anchor only), so a real bloodbath trips `verified_crowded` while a purely model-imagined crowd (zero verified anchors) still cannot — the original anti-hallucination cure preserved, the under-call cured (error direction now safe: over-call crowded, never under-call). **(4) a token-leak SCRUB** — internal evidence ids (`signal_N` / `field_N` / `coverage.*`) are banned from Explore prose by a synthesis rule + a deterministic route `scrubLeaks` backstop (which LEAVES `lane_N` / `angle_N`, legitimate structural refs). **(5) the latency model** — Stage 2a-explore moved to Haiku (a temp-0 transform); Stage 1 stays the SHARED Sonnet spine (byte-identical to Deep — the same-evidence moat that makes the two modes coherent), so Explore is a structural ~3-minute operation by design, not a bug. **THE DOCTRINAL THROUGH-LINE:** the HARSH · FAIR · TRACEABLE creed is Deep's and untouched; Explore's parallel discipline is HONEST · DIVERGENT · NON-RANKING, and this session strengthened all three — HONEST (the deflators make the labels finally agree with the disconfirmer prose), DIVERGENT (the re-eval-as-delta mirror was correctly REFUSED because variance is Explore's feature), NON-RANKING (the angle-steer killed). The V11.17 `branch_idea_text` neutrality discipline + the mode-boundary lock are UNTOUCHED — Deep still judges cold; the take-to-Deep handoff now routes through the Deep INPUT screen (review before spend) but carries the raw idea text exactly as before. **STILL OPEN (recorded, NOT a contract issue):** the FAN-READ BAND (mocked, not built — needs the selector rule that reads the fan's SHAPE from `disconfirmer_kind` / `rests_on` / readiness); the synthesis-prompt bundle (crisp `firms_up_fastest` + no `angle_N` in prose + the deferred closeable_gap re-tag fix #2); the loop thread ("Since last time" on re-explore); the deferred Explore latency (Stage-1 fork w/ an equivalence gate, the Stage1+2a merge, the synthesis trim, streaming); the save-route idempotency; the carried Deep-side items (the `DELETE /api/folders/[id]` route, the orphaned set-main route, the inert set-as-main checkbox, `onAdvance` wiring, the deferred story narrative, provenance-handoff routing + the verdict-lead VIEW-side fallback). **OLD free / proMode / hubpreview references in this document's body remain HISTORICAL.** **V9 STILL OPEN.** Lock condition UNCHANGED from V9.28/V9.29/V9.30 (score-shape guard never fires across the first 100+ evals + scorer schema stable + Phase 13 watch zones close, OR auto-lock July 15, 2026). V8-LOCKED preserved. **Amendments inventory UNCHANGED at 25** (V9.30 newest, V9.28 authoritative) — Explore-mode engine / route / frontend, refining the separately-tracked `ll2_explore_v1`, adding NO §3 DEEP output field and NO amendment to the V9 line. sharpened SCOPE to catch the stack/pipeline stated as plain facts; the span runs the COMPLETE clause to its natural boundary, single-sentence-capped, stopping at a topic shift), recall raised by the prompt, precision held by the verbatim guard. **WHAT THIS RECORDS (contract-relevant facts, since none is a contract CHANGE):** **(1) the six-part display vocabulary** (target / problem / mechanism / money / moat / scope → metric md/md/or/mo/or/tc, in `ideaParts.js`) is a DISPLAY mapping over the idea text, NOT a scorer surface — it colours which clause carries which axis on the re-eval canvas. **(2) the X-ray's "how it's won" is the engine `direction` field** (NOT Haiku) — TRACEABLE's existing handle, surfaced again, unchanged. **(3) the colour-pass `anatomy` hint** is built from the EXISTING committed diagnosis fields (`market_demand.diagnosis` / `originality.differentiation_basis_diagnosis` + `defensibility_diagnosis` / `monetization.diagnosis` / `technical_complexity.base_score_explanation`) — read, not rewritten. **(4) the change walkthrough** (`changeDiff.js` `diff` + `prompt-reeval-walkthrough.js` + the Sonnet route + `!`-markers in `DeepResultParts` / `EvaluationView`) narrates the committed V1→V2 movement per metric — a terminal explainer over finished output, non-fatal. **(5) the prompt was refined twice from real output** — first tagged only the 4 loud parts; rewrite #1 added bias-to-include + loosened moat + sharpened scope; rewrite #2 replaced "smallest span" with "the complete clause to its natural boundary" so MONEY spans the full pricing statement (and a founder's edit to the trajectory stays INSIDE the span, so the span-diff anchors). **THE DOCTRINAL THROUGH-LINE:** the HARSH · FAIR · TRACEABLE creed is untouched — this whole session is the re-eval intake + two presentation passes around the unchanged engine; Prior: V11.28, June 20, 2026 — **MY IDEAS HUB + LINEAGE VIEW — the hub redesigned (HubView React port + a family-card hover preview), the lineage view fully built out (edge score-deltas + a "what changed" chip · best-by-score glow / favorite STAR · a clickable LEAD pill · status Active/Parked/Killed · a delta-vs-parent + churn-coaching inspector · mode-filter chips + search), ROOT and LEAD DECOUPLED (the hub now ALWAYS shows the family ROOT; Lead is a visual-only badge), and the LEAD-SWITCH FLICKER killed; one ADDITIVE Supabase migration (`is_favorite` + `disposition`)** — ALL frontend / hub-orchestrator / additive-schema, touching NO §3 interpretation-surface CONTRACT, **NOT a V9.x amendment** (no §3.x DEEP surface, no score formation, no `lookup[archetype][sub_position]`, no MB selection, no `overall_score`, no scorer schema, no MO `display_score` / override-trace, no score-shape guard; the V5.0 DEEP scoring engine is BYTE-UNCHANGED in scoring terms at `bf09382` + the Arc-7→Arc-12 + LL1 + LL2 + V78 + V80 + V82 + V83 + V84 + V85 + V86 commits; `ll2_explore_v1` UNCHANGED — rendered / persisted, not redefined; the Supabase change is the FIRST schema change since the V11.19 `hub_model_v1` migration and is ADDITIVE ONLY — two columns, no drops, applied LIVE via the MCP). **WHY THIS TOUCHES NO V9 CONTRACT:** V9 governs the SCORING discipline; this session is the idea-HUB and its genealogy view — which card the hub shows per family, how the lineage renders / branches, a per-node favorite + disposition flag, and a client-state flicker fix. None of it forms, re-encodes, or reports a score, and none of it adds or amends a §3 prose surface — it is the LL3 hub MODEL's display + orchestration layer (the V11.19 / V11.20 / V11.21 family), extended. **THE LOAD-BEARING DECISION (Emre's call, recorded as the operative doctrine) — ROOT and LEAD ARE DECOUPLED:** the hub shows each family by its fixed ROOT (the origin identity, which never moves); "Lead" (`is_main_version`) is now a VISUAL-ONLY badge that lives in the lineage and changes nothing about the hub. Before this session the hub picked its per-family card as `members.find(is_main) || root`, so any `is_main` write (re-eval, branch, an inline "set as main version" button) could reshuffle the hub card — the observed bug: re-evaluating a deep child "k" made the hub show "k" instead of the family root. Pinning the hub to root fixes the whole class at the SOURCE: with the card always the root, no `is_main` caller can reshuffle it, so the bug is structurally impossible regardless of who sets the flag. **WHAT THIS RECORDS (contract-relevant facts, since none is a contract CHANGE):** **(1) the `lineage_favorite_disposition` migration (LIVE, additive)** — `ideas.is_favorite boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false` + `ideas.disposition text` (CHECK in {null, parked, killed}); `disposition` is DELIBERATELY SEPARATE from `status` (the active/archived soft-delete) so a parked/killed node STAYS VISIBLE in the lineage — a lifecycle label, never a delete. **(2) `ideas.js` decouple** — `IDEA_LIGHT_SELECT` carries `is_favorite` + `disposition`; `shapeNode` surfaces `changed_dimensions` (jsonb) + `is_favorite` + `disposition`; `updateIdea` accepts both AND delegates an `is_main:true` patch to `setMain` (SET LEAD reuses the existing PATCH, no new route); `listHub` now ALWAYS shapes the family ROOT (`byId[rootId]`, was `members.find(is_main) || byId[rootId]`) — the one line that decouples Lead from the hub. **(3) `api/ideas/[id]/route.js` (PATCH)** — whitelist widened to `is_favorite` (coerced bool), `disposition` (validated), `is_main` (only `true`, delegated). **(4) `LineageView.js`** — the full feature pass (jsonb-safe `fmtChanged`; filter + query; `bestId` auto-glow; optimistic toggleFavorite / setDisposition / setLead; clickable LEAD pill / BEST pill / favorite STAR / KILLED-PARKED tag / glow ring; edge score-deltas + a changed chip; a LEAD-VERSION + 3-chip-status + delta-vs-parent + churn-coaching inspector; filter chips + search; NO story narrative) **and the lead-switch flicker fix** — `setLead`→`updateIdea` does an optimistic `setMyIdeas` that flags the new node main WITHOUT clearing the old lead, so `myIdeas` briefly holds two mains; the reconcile effect's deps `[targetIdeaId, myIdeas]` re-fired on that churned array and re-derived a two-LEAD family until the server lineage re-fetch landed — the fix drops `myIdeas` from the deps (`[targetIdeaId]`), because after mount this view OWNS its node state and applies all local mutations optimistically. **(5) `page.js`** — SET LEAD is now the SINGLE lead-setter: the inline "set as main version" button (the original hub-flip promoter), the branch auto-promote, and `onSetAsMain` (→ no-op) are removed; with the hub root-pinned these are belt-and-suspenders for clarity rather than the fix. **(6) the "MY IDEAS HUB" REDESIGN** — `HubView.js` ported to React with a family-card hover preview (replacing the editorial STRONG/OPEN fields), rendering `listHub`'s `{folders, rough, ideas}` with `family_size`; it never touches `is_main`, so the root-pinned `listHub` is the whole story for the hub card. **THE RECORDED CONSEQUENCE (a design choice, not a surprise):** a family ROOTED in an explore (or rough) idea shows in the hub as that explore/rough card EVEN WITH deep branches — the deep work lives one click away in the lineage; this is the literal meaning of "the hub always shows the root" and is intended (root = stable family identity; lineage = where evolution + the Lead badge live). **THE DOCTRINAL THROUGH-LINE:** the HARSH · FAIR · TRACEABLE creed is untouched; this whole session is the hub/lineage presentation + orchestration skin around the unchanged engine — pinning the hub to root makes a bug-class structurally unreachable (the orchestrator face of the structural-separation lever), and a focused view owning its state post-mount (the flicker fix) are both the navigation/display authority, never the score authority. **OLD free / proMode / hubpreview references in this document's body remain HISTORICAL.** **V9 STILL OPEN.** Lock condition UNCHANGED from V9.28/V9.29/V9.30 (score-shape guard never fires across the first 100+ evals + scorer schema stable + Phase 13 watch zones close, OR auto-lock July 15, 2026). Verified on real output: the page is the SAME depth, fewer words — MORE Deep per sentence; what was cut was never analysis, only connective tissue. **WHAT THIS RECORDS (contract-relevant facts, since none is a contract CHANGE):** **(1) Risk B8 on Stage 2c** (`prompt-stage2c.js`, 1234→1263) — a new RISK LENGTH & DENSITY governor between B7 and Block C: lead ≤45w + an OPTIONAL continuation ≤30w (invalid if it adds a 2nd mechanism / re-explains / hedges); target 40–55 / ceiling 65 per risk; a per-field EVIDENCE FLOOR keyed to "every LOAD-BEARING fact" (not every fact); ABSENCE PRECISION with ROTATING shapes (held the line vs ChatGPT's single fixed "No evidence shows" default, which would template per B4). Prior: V11.25, June 19, 2026 — **THE EXECUTION BRIEF OVER-WRITING KILL — a per-field length discipline added to the Screen-3 / step-4 Handoff prompt: a Block-2 OVER-WRITING KILL fence, hard per-field CAPs, and a structural TWO-ELEMENT threshold rule; plus one rule ADDED-THEN-REVERTED (the bet see-saw cadence ban)** — this is a DISCIPLINE-TIGHTENING of the existing §3 Deep interpretation surface (the Execution Brief / Handoff prose), prompt-only, adding NO output field and changing NO wire contract, **NOT a V9.x amendment** (the brief is bottleneck-relative and constitutionally FORBIDDEN from re-scoring — it never receives numeric scores; nothing about score formation, `lookup[archetype][sub_position]`, the MB SELECTION, `overall_score`, the scorer schema, MO `display_score` / override-trace, or the score-shape guard is touched; the V5.0 DEEP scoring engine is BYTE-UNCHANGED in scoring terms at `bf09382` + the Arc-7→Arc-12 + LL1 + LL2 + V78 + V80 + V82 + V83 commits; `ll2_explore_v1` UNCHANGED; NO Supabase / route / view change). **This CLOSES the Execution-Brief over-length item V83/V11.24 flagged as next-work.** **WHY THIS TOUCHES NO V9 CONTRACT:** V9 governs SCORING discipline — `.score = lookup[archetype][sub_position]` (V9.28 authoritative), the MO `display_score` decoupling (V9.30), the score-shape guard, scorer-schema stability. The Execution Brief is the FORWARD-VOICE handoff that accepts the settled diagnosis and projects it (FIRST / NOT YET / UNTIL / THEN / WON'T COUNT); it reads prose + the binding-constraint shape, never the scores, and re-scoring is banned by its own Block 0. A length discipline on its prose fields is the furthest thing from a scoring amendment. **THE SURFACE (one Sonnet call, `claude-sonnet-4-6`, temp 0.5, over the settled diagnosis; six sentinel-delimited blocks bet → prove_next → order → wont_count → gates → handoff; rendered by `ExecutionBriefView.js`):** the Sonnet 4.5 → 4.6 switch made a latent over-writing live — each STRUCTURAL field said its one thing two-to-three times via a fixed grammar, `[core claim] — [em-dash gloss] — [significance tail]`. The contract now fences that explicitly. **THE NEW DISCIPLINE (enters §3 via the §5 Update Protocol as a fence on an existing surface, not a new surface):** **(1) THE OVER-WRITING KILL (Block 2, the gate's length edge).** Contract: a structural field states its content ONCE, at one grain, and stops — no em-dash gloss re-saying the core at finer grain, no tail narrating why the field matters; the brief's STRUCTURE (section headers, the produces/signal split, the gated order) carries significance, so a field that explains its own importance has done the structure's job in the field's words and doubled its length. Doctrine: STRUCTURAL / NAMED-DISEASE discipline over a bare word cap — the same family as TC isolation, the 2a/2b split, and the V83 verdict compressor, here applied as a fence rather than a separation because the brief's structural fields carry NO field-gravity (their jobs — "stated plainly," an artifact noun — already agree with brevity), so a named ceiling binds without a second surface. **Anchor predicates:** the cut removes the gloss and the tail and NEVER the wall-specific object (three-way calibration baked in: `bloated` → `right` → `too generic`; cut to the middle, never the third); the 4a-4f illustrations are LENGTH models (ten-to-fifteen words, wall-specific, fenced) and a field at two-to-three times its illustration has over-written; the kill governs STRUCTURAL fields only. **Forbidden predicates:** cutting to a generic object ("build the core" — specificity is load-bearing, the cut that dissolves the wall-specific noun has gone too far); applying the kill to the bet or handoff serif lines (exempt — their own one-sentence caps). **(2) HARD PER-FIELD CAPs (4b / 4c / 4d).** Contract: evidence one sentence; bar one sentence ("Enough looks like" is the bar, not a preamble); action one sentence; `produces` ONE artifact phrase with NO why-it-matters clause (an artifact phrase, not a pure noun phrase and not an explanation — "a pre-launch list of 200 organic opt-ins" passes, "…so that the launch fires into a warm audience" is the tail and is cut); signal one sentence; each won't-count entry one sentence; a firing resource/close-call clause one sentence, never a paragraph (the pileup ceiling is a LENGTH rule as much as a count rule). **Anchor predicate:** each field matches the length of its section's own illustration. **Forbidden predicate:** a count-legal field (right number of steps/entries) that is nonetheless length-illegal (each field two-to-three times its illustration). **(3) THE TWO-ELEMENT THRESHOLD RULE (4e, gates — structural, paraphrase-proof).** Contract: `revise_if` and `stop_if` are EXACTLY two elements — a cost (time / money / attempts) and the unmet bar (the specific evidence that has not landed) — and then they STOP; there is no third element; after the unmet bar the sentence ends. **Anchor predicate:** count the elements — cost + unmet bar = two, full stop. **Forbidden predicate:** any third clause after the unmet bar, WHATEVER it says (a rationale, a wall-width restatement, a cost-trend, a precedent gloss) — it is the significance tail wearing a decision label; the two elements already force the decision and the structure already carries the why. (This replaced a first-attempt phrasing-LIST ban that the Distribution `stop_if` slipped by paraphrasing — naming the STRUCTURE, not the strings, is what binds; the same lesson the rest of this contract already encodes.) **THE REVERTED RULE (recorded as the discipline's negative edge):** a 4a FORM addition named and banned the bet's see-saw cadence ("[strong axis] is real — the open question is whether [the wall], and the first move tests that"); across six regenerations the model stayed on banned cadences anyway, because cadence variety ACROSS briefs is structurally unenforceable in a stateless single call (no memory of the prior bet → the model picks the locally-natural shape every time) and is USER-INVISIBLE (one user sees one bet, which reads well). The rule was STRIPPED, not kept — 4a FORM is back to its original text. A contract rule that cannot enforce what it claims is removed, not retained: the inverse of a lock. **THE DOCTRINAL THROUGH-LINE (worth recording):** the HARSH · FAIR · TRACEABLE creed still holds on this surface, now DENSER not longer — the brief stays comprehensive (all six blocks, the full order, both fences) and stops explaining itself; "the structure carries significance, the field carries only the thing" is the operative doctrine, and it is the prose-discipline face of the same structural-over-phrasing lever the engine work keeps landing on. **OLD free / proMode / hubpreview references in this document's body remain HISTORICAL.** **V9 STILL OPEN.** Lock condition UNCHANGED from V9.28/V9.29/V9.30 (score-shape guard never fires across first 100+ evals + scorer schema stable + Phase 13 watch zones close, OR auto-lock July 15, 2026). V8-LOCKED preserved. **Amendments inventory UNCHANGED at 25** (V9.30 newest, V9.28 authoritative) — this is a §3 interpretation-surface discipline-tightening, adds NO output field and NO amendment to the V9 line. Cascade: MasterReference V83→V84 + this NarrativeContract V11.24→V11.25 + ActionQueue V26→V27. The close-call gate refines `is_close_call` REPORTING precision, not the MB selection and not any score. **The redesign shipped as commit `8a2cac1`** (committed + pushed + browser-confirmed by Emre; live); **the correction (two files) is delivered + validated this session (parse-clean + esbuild-clean), paste + commit pending.** **THE FIVE NEW §3 DEEP SURFACES (enter §3 via the §5 Update Protocol):** **(1) VERDICT-LEAD COMPRESSION ("Option B," `prompt-verdict-lead.js` + the route call).** Contract: Stage 2c's `summary` remains the FULL rich verdict (the modal); a separate isolated Haiku pass (`VERDICT_LEAD_SYSTEM_PROMPT`, `claude-haiku-4-5-20251001`, max_tokens 400, temp 0) distills the finished verdict + headline into a 3-beat (FOUNDATION / CONSTRAINT / PIVOT) ≤80-word `verdict_lead` (the card). Doctrine: PHYSICAL SEPARATION beats prompt-rule enforcement — the same lesson as the V4S9–V11 TC isolation and the Stage 2a/2b split. `summary` is the gravitational centre of 2c (the job framing + A1 + A2–A9 all pull length IN); one in-Block-A brevity rule cannot reverse that gravity, but a clean-context isolated call has nothing asking for richness, so the cap binds. **Anchor predicates:** `verdict_lead` introduces NO fact / number / source / claim not already in `summary`; it compresses, never re-judges / re-scores / softens / strengthens; non-fatal — on failure the card falls back to the rich `summary`; the modal shows the rich `summary`. **Forbidden predicates:** the compressor adding evidence (it transports the finished verdict only); making the `summary` field itself short to serve the card (that re-introduces the gravity fight — `summary` stays the rich verdict). **(2) `verdict_headline` (A11, Stage 2c, REQUIRED).** Contract: the case-truth (§1.1) stated as a verdict-SHAPE in ≤8 words — the WHAT, anchored to upstream per A2, never invented; band-family is a HINT, case-truth OVERRIDES; high templating risk ("[adjective] opportunity, [verb]-ed by [X]" is a mold-in-waiting). **Anchor predicates:** ≤8 words; traceable to the case-truth; DIVERGES from the summary's opening sentence (the headline is the WHAT, the summary opener is the WHY — they must not restate each other). **Forbidden predicates:** score restatement ("A 6.7 idea"), generic verdict ("A promising idea"), enumeration ("strong demand, weak monetization, hard build" — a scoreboard is not a shape, per A1), internal labels (D6), other-stage territory (D7). **(3) `competitive_position` tri-split (A13, Stage 2c) + per-competitor `take` (Stage 1).** Contract: `competitive_position { headline, overlap, you_win, exposed }` is the synthesis HEADER for "How your idea compares" — the ONE place the pipeline JUDGES where the idea sits against the listed competitors (drawing on the Stage 1 list + the originality packet); null when no genuine direct/adjacent rival (the view falls back to descriptive differentiation). This RESPECTS the standing boundary that Stage 1 is a constitutional REPORTER, FORBIDDEN from judging differentiation strength — the differentiation JUDGMENT lives in 2c. Stage 1's `take` is a ≤12-word NEUTRAL competitor characterization (strongest point + most relevant gap), the punchy surface form of facts already in strengths/weaknesses. **Anchor predicates:** every `competitive_position` cell traces to listed competitors + originality evidence (A2); `you_win`/`exposed` are the compressed originality-packet defensibility read; lives at LANDSCAPE altitude — must NOT restate the summary or `verdict_headline`; `take` describes the competitor only. **Forbidden predicates:** `take` framing where the idea wins or judging market viability (Stage 2's job); `competitive_position` manufacturing a wedge against a field that isn't there; the competition header re-delivering the verdict. **(4) CLOSE-CALL DECISIVENESS GATE (`is_close_call`, Stage 3).** Contract: `is_close_call` is true ONLY when the selection was genuinely hard on the CURRENT evidence — the two candidates near-parity in how much they bind RIGHT NOW, and the tiebreaker turned on a fact UNRESOLVED in the evidence; a counterfactual on a SETTLED fact ("if the founder were senior," "if the market were not regulated") is sensitivity analysis on a known input → FALSE; when in doubt, false. **Anchor predicate:** the deciding fact is genuinely uncertain in the current evidence such that a reasonable reading of the SAME evidence could have picked the runner-up. **Forbidden predicate:** firing `is_close_call` merely because two candidates fired, or on a settled-fact counterfactual. (This changes REPORTING precision only — the MB itself, the per-metric scores, and `overall_score` are untouched; outside V9 entirely.) **THE SAME-SESSION CORRECTION (paste + commit pending):** the THREE failed pre-Haiku attempts to make `summary` short had rewritten A10 ("SENTENCE ADVANCEMENT" → "+ LEAD STRUCTURE," forcing `summary` to a 3-beat ~70–100-word lead) with a coordinating A6 "LEAD APPLICATION" insert; Option B superseded that work but it was LEFT IN by accident, leaving `summary` pulled two ways. Launch-list item (2), the only remaining half of the two-mode split; Deep was done. **Architecture (locked):** keywords (+ gate) → four-source search → Stage 1 (REUSED read-only, clamped temp0/top_k1/top_p0.1) → **Stage 2a-Explore SORTER (NEW)** → Explore synthesis (open) → SSE — THREE model calls. The spine = Explore reads the SAME neutral Stage 1 evidence as Deep. **The Stage 2a-Explore sorter is the architectural heart:** Explore had been the lone RAW-EATER of Stage 1 (Deep has Stage 2a, Explore had nothing — the structural root of the run-3 non-outwardness disease, where `dominant_uncertainty = differentiation` fired ~68% even on empty niches). The sorter is the evidence-shaping middle-man Deep had and Explore was missing — SORTER-NOT-ANALYST (transforms, never generates; never holds a verdict to corrupt = spine-safe; re-shapes existing Stage 1 facts, does NOT widen coverage — coverage-widening would owe Deep re-verification). Core insight: the DUAL-FACE of each fact (Deep needs only the cap-face; Explore needs the opening-face AND the limiting-face). The route OWNS the density-classification threshold (`classifyDensityLane`) and DETERMINISTICALLY OVERWRITES each lane's `classification` (verified_crowded / emerging_unverified / mixed / sparse — categorical, NO number) so a soft model majority can't bury a real core or manufacture \"crowded\" from thin/llm evidence. **FOUR FIXED SURFACES (shipped):** Read · Angles (0–5 directions: opening + bet + disconfirmer + readiness + branch_idea_text) · **Terrain** (the V11.14 \"Open Lane\" surface, shipped as Terrain — lanes) · Next Move (dominant_uncertainty + recommendation + primary_action). The facet band was KILLED twice on real data — four surfaces are FIXED, no facet_tags. **GUARDRAIL (1) HELD — ONE coarse readiness signal per branch, NEVER a multi-axis rubric:** Explore emits `readiness` ∈ {ready_for_deep, worth_shaping, probably_thin} — a single coarse axis; no per-branch rubric was built, so Deep's verdict instrument (the §3.x scoring surfaces) was NOT rebuilt inside Explore. **GUARDRAIL (2) HELD — terminal surface is the LOOP-BACK / Next Move (save · explore · take-to-Deep), NOT a brief:** no brief-shaped thing was built for Explore; the Execution Brief stays Deep-only. **NEW DOCTRINAL LOCK — the `branch_idea_text` NEUTRALITY DISCIPLINE (spine-protection — the V11.17 contribution):** the branch object is the API between the two engines (V11.14 object model: Idea → Angle → Branch → Evaluation → Decision), and `branch_idea_text` is the take-to-Deep handoff string Deep ingests COLD. A 29-idea validation run surfaced that an expansion-shaped branch could smuggle a DEMAND VERDICT into the frozen Deep engine (\"underserved geographic regions\" — pre-loading the very answer Deep exists to judge). The lock: an expansion-shaped `branch_idea_text` NAMES its target (region / group / vertical / platform) as a FACT and NEVER characterizes that target's openness, coverage, or demand — **\"the shift is WHERE or WHO, never WHY it is open\"** — because Deep judges the SHAPE OF THE EVIDENCE and must not inherit a pre-formed verdict from Explore. It is STRUCTURAL, not a word-ban (geography is only the first costume — demographic / vertical / platform expansion smuggle the same verdict), backed by a word-guard (underserved / untapped / unmet / uncovered / overlooked / neglected) and a widened leak probe (`branch_idea_text` is a spine-critical `leak_candidate`; `dominant_uncertainty.text` + `recommendation` now scan into `warnings`, the tone surfaces the old probe was blind to). This is the mode-boundary analogue of the two V11.14 guardrails — it PROTECTS the Deep §3.x scoring contracts from Explore contamination, the same way the anti-rubric lock protects them from a rebuilt verdict instrument. A 3-idea confirm re-run came back clean (the leak cured; a same-shaped geographic-expansion angle survived verdict-free = the rule, not luck, did the work). **VALIDATION:** the 29-idea broad bank, recomputed from raw and split by the sorter's OWN classification, confirmed the cure — `emerging_unverified` ideas escape `differentiation` 9/10, while `differentiation` now CONCENTRATES where it belongs (`verified_crowded` 16/19) and is ABSENT where it was the disease (cleanest proof `couples-habits`: names direct competitors in every disconfirmer yet headlines DEMAND, because the sorter read them as UNVERIFIED). **WHY NOT A V9.x AMENDMENT:** Explore is a separate mode with its own output contract; V9.24 documents score-discipline at the cap-rule-enforcement level. **Two-stream framing locked (Type 1 / Type 2 user, both co-equal, neither subordinated):** Score = book cover (Type 1 user — sees score, doesn't read prose if score feels off); Prose = first pages (Type 2 user — reads prose, gives credit if reasoning strong). Stream A = score discipline; Stream B = prose templating with cognitive families (deferred). **Stream A patches:** A1 OVERRIDE-EXPLICIT CLAUSE (MD/MO/OR) — when scoring above what an anti-inflation rule / INVALID BASES / BINDING CAP / HEDGE DISCIPLINE would permit, prose MUST name the cap rule by identifier and state the specific packet fact that overrides it; A1 TRIGGER-BUYER MATCH amendment (MD) — buyer named must match cap-rule's specified actor (catches A3-style leak where regulatory trigger affects prescribers but cap asks about patients); A1 RULE PRECEDENCE amendment (OR) — when multiple anti-inflation rules apply, most restrictive (lowest cap value) governs (COMBINATION 4.0-5.0 < FEATURE VS PRODUCT 5.0 < VERTICAL POSITIONING 5.5 < WORKFLOW IS NOT WEDGE 6.0); A2 CAP-LANDING PRECISION (MD narrow-use + MO) — when NAMED cap fires AND no counter-anchor argues past it, score lands at cap floor (6.0) not rubric ceiling (6.5); NOT applied to OR (tiered cap landings already working calibration); A1 SCOPE clarifier ("cap does not fire merely because case has friction") — cures M2 rule-citation creep where model invoked cap language on cases where no cap was being argued past. **Anchor predicates:** when scoring above cap rule on a metric, prose names the cap rule by identifier; prose states the specific packet fact overriding the cap; when NAMED cap fires without counter-anchor on MD/MO, score lands at cap floor; OR scoring follows tiered cap landings (4.5/5.0/5.5/6.0). **Forbidden predicates:** scoring above cap without naming the cap rule and overriding fact in prose; soft engagement (describing cap-relevant friction without committing to bind OR override, landing at 6.5 between cap floor 6.0 and rubric ceiling 7.0); rule-citation creep (invoking "caps demand at the middle band" on cases where no cap rule actually fires); buyer mismatch (citing regulatory trigger affecting actor X when cap rule asks about actor Y). **Verification anchors for B10b:** MD cap-language rate (pre-A1 baseline 19%; acceptable ≤35%; fail >50% over-citation; under-citation <12% suggests soft-engagement spread); MD=6.0 cluster density (pre-A1 22/37; watch for >28-30/37 compression worsening); A3-class soft-engagement pattern frequency (≤7/37 → calibration noise, 8-15/37 → narrow A3 binding-requirement patch, >15/37 → defer to Stage 2b structural decomposition session); OR baseline preservation (tiered cap landings 4.5/5.0/5.5/6.0 hold); any new MD or MO 7.0+ leaks; M2-style well-justified cases stability. **Documented residual: "soft engagement without binding" pattern at A3** — drifted UP from 6.0 (A1 alone) to 6.5 (A1+A2) in 4/5 runs; model describes cap-relevant friction in natural language without committing to bind OR override; satisfies neither A1's enforcement (not going above 7.0) nor A2's enforcement (not formally "naming cap rule by identifier" as triggered). **Deeper structural diagnosis (token-order root cause)** — when JSON schema emits `{"scores":{"md":X}, "explanations":{"md":"..."}}`, score token emits BEFORE explanation prose; model forms holistic gestalt over packet+rubric+cap rules, emits score, then generates prose to rationalize; score+prose co-decided in one act, not sequenced as evidence→comparison→score→justification. Prompt clauses can shape prose but not underlying decision sequence. **Real structural fix (DEFERRED — conditional on B10a soft-engagement frequency):** Stage 2b output schema decomposition forcing diagnosis tokens BEFORE score token (`md_analysis: { cap_mechanisms_in_packet: [...], cap_resolutions: [...], score: X, explanation: "..." }`); token order = reasoning order; score becomes mechanically derived from prior tokens; soft-engagement loophole closes structurally not via prose discipline; session-sized work (parser changes + Stage 2c/Stage 3 input shape + schema validation + backward compatibility), not surgical patch. **Verification (8-case × 5 reruns × 2 cycles):** First cycle (A1 alone) eliminated hard leaks (A3 MD 7.5 → max 6.5, MAT2-senior OR 7.0 → max 6.5) but M2 rule-citation creep (6.5 → 6.0 across all 5 runs); second cycle (A1+A2 + SCOPE) 7/7 cases pass + both FP guards pass for first time, M2 rule-citation creep cured via SCOPE clarifier, A3 soft-engagement residual emerged. **Status:** SHIPPED — B10a VERIFICATION PENDING with decision criteria locked (see 18-may-b10a-findings.md §3.10). **V9 lock condition unchanged:** V9 transitions OPEN → LOCKED when next major surface clears (post-Stream-A B10a verification confirms scoring discipline cure landed, OR auto-lock at June 10, 2026). V8-LOCKED preserved. **V9 amendments inventory:** 19 active total (3 pre-V4S29 conditional, of which V9.1 LANDED + V9.2 + V9.3 remain conditional + 5 V4S29-queued ABSORBED into V9.17 + V9.7 ABSORBED into V9.18 + V9.19 ABSORBED into V9.23 + 2 V4S29-queued still ACTIVE V9.12/V9.13 + V9.14 + V9.15 + V9.16 + V9.17 + V9.18 + V9.20 + V9.21 NEW + V9.22 NEW + V9.23 NEW supersedes V9.19 + V9.24 NEW; V9.9 and V9.11 retired). **4 new methodology principles proposed (P17-P20) for cascade lock:** P17 (Within-profile lens as primary UX verification target — cross-profile testing answers QA questions about structural consistency; within-profile testing answers product questions about whether engine feels like seeing each idea fresh; within-profile primary for narrative-prose surfaces); P18 (Cross-case templating probe at structural session verification time — for any structural session rebuilding a surface that produces user-facing narrative prose, verification must include population-scale templating check across 20+ cases; targeted per-case verification cannot catch population-level cross-case templating by design); P19 (Score+prose co-decided at token-emission time — when JSON schema emits score before explanation, score token comes first; prose rationalizes the gestalt score; prompt clauses can shape prose but not the underlying decision sequence; for full structural control, output schema must force diagnosis tokens before score token); P20 (Justifiable variance is feature territory not bug territory — run-to-run variance on ambiguous cases between valid alternative readings is signal not noise; engine fix surfaces ambiguity, UI fix names it for user; different from cross-case dominance which is real problem). **Files modified in production this arc (3 files):** `src/lib/services/prompt-stage2c.js` (β1 + β2 + C7 patches, +49 lines net, file now 1208 lines, May 18 ship); `src/lib/services/prompt-stage-tc.js` (tcIncrementalNote + tcBase patches, +19 lines net, May 18 ship); `src/lib/services/prompt-stage2b.js` (Stream A1+A2+SCOPE patches, 452→514 lines, +62 lines net, +1287 words, May 19 ship). **Two product framings established as V4+ design intent (Emre, mid-session):** (1) Justifiable variance is feature territory, not bug territory — MB variance accepted as design behavior, Risk 3 firing-rate inconsistency re-examined through this lens, alpha variance on band-boundary cases partial coverage. Engine condition: each variant must be individually correct + well-justified + bounded. UI condition: must surface honestly. (2) Ambiguity-surfacing popup pattern — schema addition (boolean ambiguity flag + alternate-reading payload), NOT logic change; UI renders unambiguous cases normally, ambiguous cases get subtle indicator + popup with "case sat between two valid framings X and Y" + reasoning chain + tipping signals. Two related concepts: ambiguity popups (primary, inline per-case) + multi-run unified read mode (secondary, power-user). **Locked execution order (May 19, 2026) — post-Stream-A ship:** (1) **Stream A B10a verification** — NEXT immediate work, decision criteria locked at §3.10 of 18-may-b10a-findings.md; (2) **Conditional next** based on Stream A B10a outcome: Stream B prose templating session (cognitive families), OR narrow A3 binding-requirement patch + re-verify, OR Stage 2b structural decomposition session (schema change); (3) **Stage 2a calibration revisit** for MD compression — bigger work, structurally separate, deferred; (4) **Execution Plan feature planning session**; (5) **Execution Plan feature build.** Pre-launch infrastructure work still deferred. V4+ product features tracked: ambiguity popups (primary), multi-run unified read mode (secondary). **Closure cascade for this session (3 docs updated + 1 new tracking doc):** (i) NarrativeContract V11.2 → V11.3 (V9.21 + V9.22 + V9.23 + V9.24 amendments integrated, V9.19 absorbed into V9.23); (ii) MasterReference V61 → V62; (iii) NEW `18-may-b10a-findings.md` tracking document created as append-only handoff doc covering full arc from May 18 B10a to Stream A ship.)

**Updated:** May 21, 2026 (V8 still LOCKED — V4S30 Stage 2b schema externalization + V4S31 two-call physical separation + V4S32 Prosecutor + Repair quality-control layer SHIPPED, May 19-21 arc, production V4S32 LIVE on idealoopcore.com as of May 21. NO V8 contract sections changed — V9.25 + V9.26 + V9.27 are additions to V9 OPEN, not modifications of V8 sections. **§3.X Stage 2b internal scoring discipline substantially extended** (from V9.15/V9.24 base) with V9.25 schema externalization language + V9.26 two-call physical separation language. **NEW §3.Y Stage 2b QC-layer boundary discipline** added with V9.27 amendment language documenting prosecutor + repair architecture, QC verdict enum, per-metric quality_control metadata field, payload-level quality_control_summary, strip-before-Stage-2c pattern, DOUBLE_FAIL UX policy, STAGE2B_QC_MODE feature flag, and prosecutor_prompt_version forward-compat hook. **V9.25 + V9.26 + V9.27 are ELEVENTH through THIRTEENTH V9.x amendments with concrete production deployment** — all three shipped May 19-21, contract language drafted at amendment time per V9.15/V9.16/V9.17/V9.18/V9.19/V9.20/V9.21/V9.22/V9.23/V9.24 precedent. §9 V9 amendments tracking updated. **The V4S30 → V4S31 → V4S32 arc context:** Per V11.3's locked decision tree at §3.10 of 18-may-b10a-findings.md, Stream A B10a verification was the next move. Emre cost-reframed: "if we run B10a then end up doing Stage 2b structural anyway, we test twice — 2x cost." ChatGPT proposed Option B (internal adjudication fields, not user-facing). Claude recommended Path 3 (Option B). V4S30 implemented Option B. V4S30's hard fail on override frequency (~40% stuck) forced V4S31's two-call physical separation. V4S31's structural success (override 40% → 3%) AND structural failure (17% spike rate unchanged across V4S29 + V4S30 + V4S31) forced the recognition that three architectural moves all hitting the same residual = irreducible single-judgment stochasticity. V4S32 broke the floor by changing mechanism class: adversarial audit + constrained repair instead of more constraint layers on generation. **V9.25 amendment — V4S30 Stage 2b schema externalization (NEW, May 20, 2026, locked from V4S30 ship).** Extends §3.X Stage 2b internal scoring discipline (V9.15 base + V9.24 cap-rule enforcement). Externalizes adjudication decisions into Stage 2b output. **Schema additions per metric (MD/MO/OR):** `score_adjudication` object with sub-fields `positive_basis` (anchor fact citation + metric_relevance + packet_fact_cited), `applicable_rules` (array of cap rule identifiers that apply or could apply), `primary_limiting_rule_id` (cap rule with strongest case for binding), `resolution` (closed enum: `binds` / `overridden` / `not_applicable`), `override_evidence` (object when resolution=overridden: packet_fact_cited + trigger_buyer_match_verified + chain_of_reasoning), `score_basis` (closed enum: 10 patterns covering cap-bound, cap-overridden, no-cap-fired, evidence-thin, and combinations). **Per-metric rule_id enums:** MD (8 rule ids covering INVALID_BASES, HARD_NEWS_DISCIPLINE, REGULATED_TRIGGER, etc.); MO (8 rule ids including HEDGE_DISCIPLINE); OR (9 rule ids including COMBINATION, FEATURE_VS_PRODUCT, VERTICAL_POSITIONING, WORKFLOW_IS_NOT_WEDGE). **MO co-fire cascade language** documents how multiple MO rules interact when several apply simultaneously. **Walk-all-candidates prompt-level not emitted** in output (avoids `reason_not_applicable` templating surface × 25 per eval per ChatGPT correction). **Naming corrections incorporated per ChatGPT review rounds:** `cap_check` → `score_adjudication` (bilateral, not negative-only); `score_basis: emit vs derive` → `emit` (intermediate commitment matters in token order, preserves V9.15 token-order discipline); DOMAIN_FLAG_MD addition rejected per Claude pushback (A3's cap is REGULATED, not a parallel taxonomy). **Anchor predicates:** Stage 2b output includes `score_adjudication` object for each metric; adjudication decisions are externalized as structured fields not embedded in prose alone; resolution enum is closed; rule_id enums per metric are closed; score_basis enum closed at 10 patterns. **Forbidden predicates:** prose-only adjudication without structural fields populated; resolution outside closed enum; `applicable_rules` with rule_ids outside the per-metric closed list; `score_basis` outside the 10-pattern enum. **Verification anchors for B10b:** override frequency on adjudication-eligible cases (V4S30 baseline ~40% — too high, indicates rationalization layer not enforcement layer); resolution enum coverage 100% (all metrics emit valid enum value); rule_id enum coverage 100%; score_basis enum coverage 100%; co-fire cascade correctness on MO cases with multiple applicable rules; trigger_buyer_match_verified boolean correctness on REGULATED_TRIGGER cases. **Diagnosis at V4S30 verification:** override frequency stuck at ~40%, watch zones 1/4 closed. Three distinct failure modes — A3 override rationalization (cap correctly identified, `trigger_buyer_match_verified=true` emitted with chain-of-reasoning bridging the actor gap; same disease moved into `override_evidence`); MAT3-tna walk-all skipping (`applicable_rules=[]` when HEDGE_DISCIPLINE-eligible content present); M2 rule precedence (consistently picks VERTICAL_POSITIONING cap 5.5 when COMBINATION 4.0-5.0 applies — systematic). Schema externalization made the disease visible in structured form but didn't reduce it — single-call generation can rationalize structured fields the same way it rationalized prose. **Status:** SHIPPED — partial structural win, override frequency floor demonstrated single-call irreducibility. **Methodology principle locked from V4S30 verification:** Data-collection greps need same rigor as verification thresholds — validate against real output before claiming a number. The Stream B false-zero measurement (claimed 0% rates because regexes were calibrated to May 18 instantiations not actual cognitive template) was caught by Emre, not Claude. Re-grep'd properly produced MD "Interview N" 51%, MD "to identify what specific" 46%, MO "Run a N-X pilot" 63%, OR "Build proprietary X" 69%. P21 in P17-P20 cascade. **V9.26 amendment — V4S31 Two-call physical separation (NEW, May 20-21, 2026, locked from V4S31 ship).** Extends §3.X Stage 2b internal scoring discipline. Replaces single-call Stage 2b with two physically separated calls. **Architecture:** Call 1 = Stage 2b-Adj (`prompt-stage2b-adj.js`, 569 lines) emits `score_adjudication` ONLY (no scores, no explanations) — adjudication decisions made under structural-input pattern with JSON.stringify locked input from Stage 2a + Stage 1. Call 2 = Stage 2b-Score (`prompt-stage2b-score.js`, 327 lines) receives Stage 2a evidence packets + Stage 1 + Stage 2b-Adj output as structural input, emits scores + explanations + evidence_strength. Code-side score clamping via `deriveExpectedScoreRange(adjudication)` helper in route.js validates Call 2 scores against Call 1's adjudication decisions (resolution + rule_id + score_basis → expected score range); out-of-range scores get clamped to band-floor with warning logged. **Downstream pass-through DEFERRED to Step 2:** Stage 2c and Stage 3 currently receive ev with `score_adjudication` stripped (preserves V9.15/V9.17 strip-before-Stage-2c pattern). Step 2 work would pass adjudication forward with orientation language preventing D6 label leakage (REGULATED/ENTERPRISE/etc as prose tokens) + D7 stage-boundary erosion — deferred until Stage 2c and Stage 3 prompts can be amended to consume structural adjudication without contaminating their narrative output. **Anchor predicates:** Stage 2b is physically split into Call 1 + Call 2; Call 1 emits adjudication only; Call 2 receives Call 1's adjudication as structural input; code-side clamping validates Call 2 scores against Call 1's adjudication; `score_adjudication` is stripped before Stage 2c by default. **Forbidden predicates:** Stage 2b emits scores in same call that emits adjudication (single-call rationalization pattern); Call 2 receives raw narrative adjudication instead of structured fields; downstream stages receive `score_adjudication` without explicit pass-through amendment (Step 2 territory). **Verification anchors for B10b:** override frequency drop (V4S30 ~40% → V4S31 ~3%, 37pp architectural success signal); resolution-score consistency 100% (clamping interface clean); spike rate at borderline cases (V4S31 verification: 6/35 = 17%, unchanged from V4S29 and V4S30 — irreducibility signal); latency budget (single-call ~50-60s → two-call ~70-80s, within budget); MD templating regression watch (V4S31 verification: "Interview N" 51 → 80%, "to identify what specific" 46 → 89% — Call 2 leans on worked examples, +43pp regression flagged for H4 anti-template clause); OR templating improvement ("Build proprietary X" 69 → 29%); L2 MARKETPLACE_MO tag fabrication concentration (4 of 7 citation failures = same case-rule pair, indicates Stage 2a packet variance contributing). **Documented residual: 17% spike rate floor.** V4S29 rigor template 17%. V4S30 schema externalization 17%. V4S31 physical separation 17%. Three architectural moves all hit same residual — diagnosed as irreducible stochasticity of single semantic judgment on borderline cases. Each architectural constraint layer adds less than the previous (diminishing returns curve). **Status:** SHIPPED — partial structural win (override frequency cured), structural fail (spike floor unchanged) forcing recognition that the next move must be a mechanism change not another constraint layer. **Methodology principle locked from V4S31:** Mechanism change > careful generation when on diminishing-returns curve. P22 in P17-P22 cascade. **Justifiability beats consistency as success bar** — tested all 6 V4S31 spikes against Emre's bar ("if the prose is sound I don't care about 7.5 spikes 1/5 as long as our prose is not templating and well-justifiable") — none passed. The 17% spike rate WAS a real problem under the justifiability bar even though it was low under the consistency bar. P23. **V9.27 amendment — V4S32 Prosecutor + Repair quality-control layer (NEW, May 21, 2026, locked from V4S32 production ship).** **NEW §3.Y Stage 2b QC-layer boundary discipline** added — the first interpretation-surface boundary contract for a downstream-of-Stage-2b stage that isn't Stage 2c or Stage 3. Documents adversarial audit + constrained repair as a new architectural layer between Stage 2b-Score and Stage 2c. **Architecture:** Sequential layer between Stage 2b-Score and Stage 2c (not parallel — Stage 2c reads scores + explanations and must reflect post-repair values, so Stage 2c receives the post-QC ev). Per-metric parallelization within the layer (MD/MO/OR independent — Promise.all for prosecutor calls, repair calls, re-prosecution calls; wall latency = max(metric) not sum(metrics)). Six-phase orchestration: (1) trigger evaluation (sync, pure function); (2) prosecutor calls in parallel for triggered metrics; (3) repair calls in parallel for FAIL verdicts; (4) re-prosecution calls in parallel for repaired outputs; (5) merge results into ev with per-metric quality_control field; (6) build payload-level quality_control_summary. **Trigger logic (active at launch):** `high_score` (score ≥ 7.0 — spike territory, UNGROUNDED_HIGH_SCORE + INVALID_ANCHOR catches); `overridden` (resolution === "overridden" from V9.25 adjudication — A3-class disease catches); `empty_rules_with_high_score` (applicable_rules.length === 0 AND score ≥ 6.5 — walk-all-skip risk on MAT3-tna senior, MAT2-beg disease catches). **Trigger log-only at launch:** `mid_band_anchor_risk` (regex/substring match on positive_basis content — boolean flag, no prosecution call; offline sample-prosecute later if production data shows catch rate is meaningful). **Skip cases (always SKIPPED_NO_TRIGGER without calling prosecutor):** score < 6.0 (no overconfidence to catch); applicable_rules non-empty AND resolution === "binds" AND score === cap_floor_value (textbook clean cap landing). **Verdict enum (6 values, per ChatGPT review correction):** SKIPPED_NO_TRIGGER (triggers evaluated, none fired — not logged to Supabase per design); QC_UNAVAILABLE (technical failure timeout/parse/5xx — logged for operational visibility); PASS (clean prosecution); BORDERLINE (close call, candidate for future popup feature surfacing); FAIL_REPAIRED (caught flaw, repair landed clean, re-prosecution PASS, score + explanation + score_adjudication replaced in ev, original_score preserved in quality_control metadata); DOUBLE_FAIL (caught flaw, repair attempted, re-prosecution also FAIL — original ev preserved unchanged, marked in metadata). **Repair regenerates score_adjudication too** (not just score + explanation) — otherwise downstream (M3 when shipped, popup feature, etc.) would read a stale adjudication. **Strip-before-Stage-2c pattern (matching V9.15/V9.17 + V9.26 adjudication strip):** Strip `quality_control` from ev before stringifying for Stage 2c input. Stage 2c shouldn't reason about it. Restore at final assembly so the frontend payload includes it. **Per-metric quality_control field on ev:** prosecutor_verdict (one of the 6 enum values); triggers_fired (array of trigger names); flaw_category (INVALID_ANCHOR / OMITTED_LIMITING_FACT / HYPOTHESIS_AS_PROOF / UNGROUNDED_HIGH_SCORE / null); repair_attempted (bool); repair_succeeded (bool); original_score (only when FAIL_REPAIRED); close_call_framing (only when BORDERLINE); prosecutor_latency_ms; repair_latency_ms. **Payload-level quality_control_summary:** qc_mode (off | log_only | repair); checked_metrics (count where prosecutor was called); repaired_metrics; borderline_metrics; double_fail_metrics; qc_unavailable_metrics; total_qc_latency_ms; qc_layer_version 'v1.0'; quality_failure (true when 2+ metrics DOUBLE_FAIL). **Feature flag STAGE2B_QC_MODE = off | log_only | repair, default 'repair'** per launch decision (Emre solo-testing — log_only doesn't earn its place when no real users exist). **Stage 2c boundary rule (sharper per ChatGPT review):** Stage 2c never sees QC metadata. Stage 2c eventually may see repaired adjudication (when V4S31 Step 2 ships M3 downstream pass-through). Stage 2c never sees failed/prosecutor-internal details (verdicts, fatal flaws, invalid_anchor citations, triggers). Anything Stage 2c receives is the repaired ev with `quality_control` stripped. **Anchor predicates:** Prosecutor + Repair layer sits between Stage 2b-Score and Stage 2c sequentially; prosecutor is triggered only on metrics meeting active trigger criteria; repair regenerates score + explanation + score_adjudication on FAIL verdicts; re-prosecution validates repairs before merge; DOUBLE_FAIL preserves original ev unchanged; quality_control metadata is stripped before Stage 2c and restored at final assembly; STAGE2B_QC_MODE feature flag gates the entire layer (off bypasses entirely, log_only runs prosecutor without mutating ev, repair is full production behavior). **Forbidden predicates:** prosecutor runs on metrics that don't meet trigger criteria (cost waste); repair regenerates score + explanation but leaves score_adjudication stale (downstream contamination); Stage 2c sees quality_control metadata or prosecutor-internal flaws (boundary violation); repaired ev mixes with original ev on DOUBLE_FAIL (untrusted-content ship); feature flag bypassed in production without explicit decision. **Verification anchors for V4S32 monitoring (post-launch, not B10b):** prosecutor trigger rate (% of metrics where prosecutor called — V4S31 sample: MD + MO + OR ≈ 30-40% trigger rate on high-stakes ideas); prosecutor FAIL rate (% of prosecuted metrics returning FAIL — B10a probe: 10%); overall FAIL rate (% of ALL metrics ending FAIL_REPAIRED — production-relevant number); repair success rate (% of FAILs where re-prosecution PASSes — B10a probe: 100%, 21/21); DOUBLE_FAIL rate (% of FAILs where re-prosecution also FAILs — B10a probe: 0%, watch for production drift, promote to UI if exceeds 5% sustained over 2-week window); QC_UNAVAILABLE rate (% of prosecutions hitting technical failure — outage signal if exceeds ~2%). **DOUBLE_FAIL UX policy LOCKED (V1):** Say nothing to users; log everything to stage2b_qc_events Supabase table; set 5% promote-to-UI threshold over 2-week window; per-metric DOUBLE_FAIL ships original with internal flag only (no "could not be verified" UI in V1); multi-metric DOUBLE_FAIL (2+ of 3) flags quality_failure: true for manual review only — NO automatic credit return in V1 (probe data shows path rarely fires; revisit post-launch with real rates). Philosophically aligned with surfacing uncertainty (Option B/C of the UX spectrum) but V1 isn't time to introduce a UI concept users have never seen alongside three-screen architecture + Paddle + onboarding + landing page launches. **Prosecutor Evolution (PE) forward-compatibility:** `prosecutor_prompt_version` column on `stage2b_qc_events` table — when feedback loop ships (PE1-PE5 post-EP), version bumps to v1.1, v1.2 etc. allow A/B comparison of prompt iterations. **Files shipped V4S32 (6 production + 1 migration):** `src/lib/services/prompt-stage2b-prosecutor.js` (263 lines, calibrated B10a v2 prompt with adjudication awareness — receives `score_adjudication` per metric as primary structural input, richer than B10a probes had); `src/lib/services/prompt-stage2b-repair.js` (233 lines, regenerates score + explanation + score_adjudication; recommended_action enum); `src/lib/services/stage2b-qc-triggers.js` (196 lines, pure sync trigger evaluation); `src/lib/services/stage2b-qc-orchestrator.js` (569 lines, 6-phase orchestration plus strip/restore helpers); `src/lib/services/log-qc-events.js` (67 lines, fire-and-forget Supabase logger); modified `src/app/api/analyze-pro/route.js` (1088 lines total, V4S31 + V4S32 integration: two-call Stage 2b orchestration + QC layer + extended strip/restore block matching V9.26 adjudication strip pattern + evaluation_id via crypto.randomUUID() + quality_control_summary in analysis payload + analysis._pro.evaluation_id for frontend join key). **Supabase migration shipped May 21, 2026:** `stage2b_qc_events` table (25 columns including evaluation_id + metric + prosecutor_verdict + flaw_category + triggers_fired + original_score + final_score + prosecutor_latency_ms + repair_latency_ms + reprosecution_latency_ms + reprosecution_verdict + prosecutor_prompt_version + original_explanation + repaired_explanation + invalid_anchor_cited + timestamp + others) + 4 helper views (v_stage2b_recent_repairs, v_stage2b_double_fails, v_stage2b_qc_rates, v_stage2b_double_fail_rates with weekly aggregation); all 4 views set `security_invoker = true` post-migration per Supabase Security Advisor (RLS-aware caller permissions inheriting underlying table's service-role-only access). **Production verification (May 21, 2026):** Migration applied + Security Advisor warnings cleared via `ALTER VIEW ... SET (security_invoker = true)` on all 4 views. Code deployed via git commit + push, Vercel auto-deploy. Diagnostic log gated behind `DEBUG_V4S32_TRIGGERS` env var so production stays quiet by default. **Production smoke results:** Brokerage idea (vertical CRM for independent insurance brokerages, high-MD market scenario) — local run produced MD repaired 7.5 → 6.0 (PASS verdict on re-prosecution, repair landed clean) + MO DOUBLE_FAIL (re-prosecution also caught flaw in repair, original 7.5 kept). Production run produced same idea — MD DOUBLE_FAIL kept 7.5 + MO DOUBLE_FAIL kept 7.5 (different stochasticity, same architecture working — re-prosecution rejected both repairs). IdeaLoop Core dogfood eval on production — MD 6.0 / MO 6.0 / OR 6.0 / TC 6.0 / Overall 6.0, zero QC events logged (correctly SKIPPED_NO_TRIGGER for all three Stage-2b-eligible metrics — no score ≥ 7.0, no override, no empty rules with score ≥ 6.5). Statistical suspicion on four-flat-6.0 investigated — diagnosed as either (a) genuine engine output for meta-product the model defaults defensively on, (b) internally balanced description landing metrics near rubric midpoint, (c) potential Stage 2c synthesis quirk normalizing TC to MD/MO/OR — none are V4S32 issues since V4S32 didn't fire on the eval. **The 17% spike floor is no longer a floor.** It's now a class of failure with defined detection mechanism (prosecutor), defined correction mechanism (repair), and validated success rates across scales: V4S31 prosecutor 5/6 = 83% spike recall + 2 anchor catches on capped-good runs; V4S31 repair 7/7 = 100% repair success, Δscore mean 1.14; B10a prosecutor sweep 23/231 = 10% with clean per-band calibration (0% FAIL at 3.5-4.5, 5% at 5-5.5, 19% at 6-6.5, 100% at 7-7.5); B10a repair 21/21 = 100% repair success, Δscore mean 0.52, 0 coherence issues. **Methodology principle locked from V4S32:** Convergent independent solutions are strong signal. Claude proposed the prosecutor + repair architecture from one angle; ChatGPT independently arrived at the same idea from a different angle and called it "prosecutor" — sharper than Claude's first version (conditional triggering, three verdicts including BORDERLINE, adversarial framing, three-stage separation). When two assistants arrive at the same architectural answer from different angles, the convergence is evidence the design is structurally correct rather than artifact of one assistant's training. **Updated:** June 4, 2026 (V8 still LOCKED — Arc 7: code-side MO DISPLAY score + 12b override trace SHIPPED to production. **V9.30 NEW — the FIRST V9.x amendment that moves a scoring computation into code** (the V11.6/V11.7 "becomes a V9.30 amendment AT SHIP TIME" forecast, realized), but narrower than forecast: it is **DISPLAY-only, so V9.28 stays UNMODIFIED** — `.score` is still the model-emitted `lookup[archetype][sub_position]`; the code value is a separate decoupled `display_score`. **What shipped (`scoring.js` + `route.js`, committed + pushed by Emre):** (a) `computeMoDisplayScore` / `computeMoScoreDiagnostic` in `scoring.js` compute a finer MO score from the committed `_internal.sub_position_predicates` (recompute sum-from-components — cures `G_ARITH_SUM` for the display value — apply the two prompt overrides, interpolate within the band); `route.js` sets `ev.monetization.display_score` at FINAL assembly (after overall_score / Stage 2c / Stage 3, after the `_internal` restore), frontend renders `display_score ?? score`; a CONSISTENCY GUARD falls back to coarse `.score` whenever code's recomputed bucket disagrees with the model's declared `sub_position`. (b) **12b** — `computeMoOverrideTrace` is the SINGLE source for MO's two bucket overrides (PRIORITY_PULL + the arithmetically-unreachable GLOBAL_SP_CAP), consumed by both the display score and the trace so they cannot drift; `route.js` writes explicit `_internal.override_applied {rule, arithmetic_bucket, final_bucket, trigger}` (or `null`) at assembly; computed from SP values only, it never reads or rewrites the model's declared `sub_position` (no silent relabeling — the explain-feature must see the mechanism); downstream reads `effective_bucket = override_applied?.final_bucket ?? sub_position`. **Decoupling = the risk-free shape V11.7 specified:** `.score` and ALL downstream behavior are provably unchanged — source-read confirmed `calculateOverallScore`, Stage 2c band gates (key off `overall_score` 5.0/6.5), and Stage 3 (`MD/MO < 5.0` modifier) all read `.score`; the fine value is out of every feedback loop. **Full code-CANONICAL migration (code owns `.score`) → investigated → RED, NOT pursued:** (1) ~27% of cases show a NON-rule-shaped disagreement between the model's declared bucket and its committed SP-sum — identical (SP-B, mechanism, strength) signatures land in different buckets because the model applies a binding-constraint pull toward lower beyond the strict PRIORITY_PULL trigger; this is the anti-inflation moat, and code-canonical would override it by fiat and INFLATE exactly those cases; (2) MO run-to-run variance is dominated by **upstream Stage 2a packet divergence** (rfull: 13/15 same-case reruns moved the MO bucket, packet VARIED 15/15) which code cannot touch (code computes from SP values that track the packet), so migration buys ZERO stability. That movement is the accepted explain-the-difference evidence-tracking, NOT scorer noise (CON-MO-B 5.4→5.4→6.0 because run-3's packet surfaced broader competitor corroboration → SP-C narrow→broad → sum 1→4 → middle). **Bounded doctrine LOCKED: code is the DISPLAY authority, not the SCORE authority** — V9.28's mechanical-lookup `.score` stays canonical; code adds fine resolution ONLY where evidence + arithmetic agree, and otherwise shows the model's coarse score. **MD + OR code-side display → DECLINED:** the MO trick delivers only where the compressed cluster's `sub_position_sum` VARIES; MD's A4 wall is 18×sum=2 (interpolation inert exactly where the compression is → resolution is multi-dimensional → PROSE, per V9.28/V11.6), and OR's dominant cluster is 16×sum=−1 honest-equivalence (spreading manufactures false distinction). The mechanism self-protects (constant-sum cluster → all map to one fine value → cannot fake precision), so it is safe-but-pointless there. The per-metric display answer is the specific answer for the one metric (MO) whose resolution is sum-shaped, NOT a template. **12b (forecast as V5.9) → LANDED here.** **12a (V5.8) → PARKED** — the real fix (MD always emits a complete `_internal`) can only live in the model/prompt (the fragile prompt-nudge class, reverted); code can only guarantee structural presence + honest degradation, not recover the missing SP judgment; it pays off only once the explain-difference feature (M2) is built (deferred), and the MD-specific ~4% miss-rate root cause (hypothesis UNCONFIRMED: MD's `_internal` is the heaviest of the three → truncated under output pressure) is banked for that session. **The V5.5 `direction`-prose-surfacing design remains DESIGNED-NOT-BUILT** (V11.6 forward note) and would be a SEPARATE later amendment when it ships. **Anchor predicates (V9.30):** MO `display_score` is computed in code at final assembly and NEVER overwrites `.score`; frontend renders `display_score ?? score`; the consistency guard falls back to coarse on bucket disagreement; `_internal.override_applied` is the single explicit record of a fired bucket override, computed from committed SP values, with `sub_position` left exactly as the model emitted it; `computeMoOverrideTrace` is the single source of the override rules (the display score and the trace cannot diverge). **Forbidden predicates:** code overwriting the canonical `.score` (it stays the V9.28 lookup value); silently relabeling `sub_position` to reconcile an override (must be explicit); a `display_score` that contradicts the committed bucket / prose (the guard prevents it by falling back to coarse); applying the MO display trick to MD or OR (their compressed clusters are constant-sum — inert or dishonest). **Empirics (clean june328 baseline, 26 MO):** fallback 38.5% (all guard_mismatch), max delta 0.6, crosses_5 = 0, distinct scores 9→13 (+4 — the 6.0 and 5.4 piles spread); GLOBAL_SP_CAP found arithmetically unreachable (spA≤1 ⟹ max sum 4 = middle) so PRIORITY_PULL is the only live override (fired 0× across the 26+49-case runs — rare; the 2/204 defect cells were the larger June 2 audit); 17/17 display-score regression + 8/8 trace tests. **V9 STILL OPEN.** Lock condition UNCHANGED from V9.28/V9.29 (score-shape guard never fires across first 100+ evals + scorer schema stable + Phase 13 watch zones close, OR auto-lock July 15, 2026). V8-LOCKED preserved. **V9 amendments inventory: 25 active total** (the 24 from V11.7 + V9.30 NEW; **V9.28 remains the authoritative scoring discipline, UNMODIFIED** — V9.30 is an additive display+trace amendment, not a change to V9.28's `.score = lookup` contract; V9.29 unmodified). **Methodology: P29-in-practice realized** — the fine+traceable corner reached via code-side derivation, but bounded to DISPLAY (the score itself stays model-judgment because bucket placement carries judgment the arithmetic doesn't capture). **First engine code shipped since V5.0.** **Closure cascade (3 living docs):** (i) NarrativeContract V11.7 → V11.8 (this entry — V9.30 NEW; §9 amendment tracking adds V9.30); (ii) MasterReference V66 → V67; (iii) ActionQueue V9 → V10 (Arc 7 + 12b DONE + 12c PARTIALLY DONE + 12a PARKED + new frontend item V5.11 + change-log V10). **Updated:** June 4, 2026 (V8 still LOCKED — MD/MO scoring-resolution investigation; MO in-prompt fine table + MD `demand_shape` marker BUILT → live-28-run FAILED → REVERTED; **production byte-for-byte unchanged**. **NO V8 contract sections changed, and NO V9.x amendment is created — nothing shipped.** V9.28 remains the AUTHORITATIVE scoring discipline, unmodified; V9.29 unmodified. This entry is a forward-note + the resolution of a previously-deferred V11.6 item, recorded so the next chat inherits the finding. **What was investigated:** whether MD/MO/OR can carry finer within-band scores that move with the prose + internal logic on current evidence — re-opening the V11.6 "REJECTED alternatives" forward note (post-lookup interpolation REJECTED; more sub_position buckets 3→4-5 DEFERRED). **Per-metric orderability (two corpora, 56-run + two 28-runs):** MD ~73% INCOMPARABLE (genuinely multi-axis — Pull = pain_intensity + current_behavior + trigger; Capture = target_specificity + capturable_density + friction_survival; a single finer scalar would manufacture false rankings); MO 62% orderable (single-axis gradient the `sub_position_sum` already captures); OR 94% orderable + a 153-pair honest-equivalence floor at 1.0 `no_defensibility_component` (OR is DONE — forcing spread = fake distinction). Evidence-locked: `current_behavior` should be FLAT-TIER (top three behaviors one tier) — the only ordering under which the MD grouping holds; record for any future MD predicate-point work. **What was BUILT then REVERTED (production never saw it):** (a) MO sum-resolution fine table — `prompt-stage-mo.js` per-archetype table keyed on `sub_position_sum` replacing the 3-anchor `DECIMAL LOOKUP`, anchors preserved, overrides composed, `v50-gates.js` given an `MO_SCORE_TABLE` branch; replay-verified (9→13 distinct, shift ≤0.40). (b) MD `demand_shape` internal marker — `prompt-stage-md.js` Section 4B computing pull/capture/shape_type from the 6 demand predicates (flat-tier `current_behavior`), with a CONDITIONAL `diagnosis` clause firing ONLY on strong/thin corners (`pull_strong_capture_thin` / `capture_strong_pull_thin`), banned-pattern fenced (no "pull"/"capture"/"demand shape" as named axes; no `<word>-pull`/`<word>-capture`; no fixed scaffold — banned examples only, ZERO positive example sentences per the P15 asymmetric-danger-of-examples lesson), scalar/archetype/sub_position/lookup byte-untouched. **The decisive live 28-run (fixture mode, local, NO deploy):** the MO fine table FAILED in execution — **12/26 cases (~46%) emitted `score` ≠ `lookup[archetype][declared sub_position_sum]`, 11 off by ≥0.2.** The model can't reliably index a dense 9-cell grid, AND the pre-existing `G_ARITH_SUM` (declared `sub_position_sum` ≠ SP-A+SP-B+SP-C) errors now translate straight into wrong scores — the 3-anchor system was ROBUST because its coarse buckets absorbed those errors, the fine table is FRAGILE because every sum maps to a distinct score. MD `demand_shape`: computed on 100% of cases with `_internal`, sensible distribution, NO enum-leakage in prose (V9.28 enum-leakage forbid held — the 2 flagged were substring false-positives), but the conditional clause fired on ~0 cases (near-inert) + one shape_type miscompute — safe, no regression, no visible user-facing effect. **REVERTED `prompt-stage-md.js`, `prompt-stage-mo.js`, and the `v50-gates.js` MO branch to known-good originals** (`node --check` clean; original `DECIMAL LOOKUP` restored; 0 `demand_shape`/`MO_SCORE_TABLE` mentions). `route.js` untouched. **RESOLUTION of the V11.6 deferred item (this is the durable contract-relevant finding):** finer within-band scoring is **CODE-SIDE-ONLY** — an in-prompt fine table is fragile (the model fails the clerical arithmetic; coarse buckets are load-bearing noise-absorption). The V11.6 "more sub_position buckets 3→4-5 DEFERRED" line is SUPERSEDED: more in-prompt buckets is the wrong, fragile mechanism. The V11.6 interpolation-offset REJECTION still stands. **The design triangle (P29 — methodology principle locked):** {fine-grained scores, evidence-traceable justification, LLM-only execution} — pick two. IdeaLoop has traceable + LLM-only (coarse robust evaluator). The fine corner requires code-side deterministic scoring from committed model judgments; generalizes V9.28's mechanical-lookup discipline + P25 one level deeper to the arithmetic-execution layer (keep deterministic arithmetic in CODE, not the LLM). **Per-metric verdict LOCKED:** OR done; MD scalar-stable + genuinely multi-dimensional (surface shape in PROSE conditionally, never the scalar, on current evidence; the MD two-axis case needs ~80–150 DISTINCT ideas run once — the orderability numbers came from corpora-WITH-reruns — before the Capture axis firms up); MO fine resolution real but reachable only code-side. **FORWARD NOTE — code-side per-metric fine scoring (DESIGNED-NOT-BUILT, explicitly NOT a V9.x amendment; ActionQueue V5.10):** move per-metric score derivation into `scoring.js` (precedent: V4S28 B8 §2 α-formula change already computes the overall score code-side). Model commits SP-A/B/C LEVELS (already in `_internal.sub_position_predicates.{spA,spB,spC}` with `level` + numeric `value`); CODE computes sum-from-components (cures `G_ARITH_SUM`) + overrides + fine table. **Decouple** — derive a coarse score (feeds Stage 2c/3, behavior provably unchanged) + a fine score (display only, out of feedback loops) = fine + traceable + risk-free, no 2c-seam ripple. Insertion point: `route.js` after `const mo = stageMoResult.monetization || {}` (line 561), before the score-shape guard; best shape = prompt reverts to robust 3-anchor as coarse fallback, code computes the authoritative fine value. **When this ships it touches `scoring.js` + `route.js` (a scoring-mechanism change, NOT a scorer-prose-contract change), but it shifts V9.28's anchor predicate "each scorer emits numeric `score` as `lookup[archetype][sub_position]`"** — the score would become CODE-derived from committed predicate levels rather than model-emitted (still equal to the lookup value, but computed downstream). That shift becomes a real V9.30+ amendment AT SHIP TIME and re-opens the cascade; until then V9.28 stands unmodified. Pre-req: confirm exactly what Stage 2c + Stage 3 read (per-metric `.score` / band / overall). **MD `demand_shape` design preserved (DESIGNED-BUILT-AND-REVERTED) for a future PROSE-surfacing revisit** — pairs with the V11.6 V5.5 `direction`-surfacing forward note; revisit as prose (not scalar) once MD two-axis is firmed on distinct-idea data. **V9 STILL OPEN.** Lock condition UNCHANGED from V9.28/V9.29: V9 → LOCKED when V5.0 production data confirms (a) score-shape guard never fires across first 100+ evaluations, (b) scorer output schema stable at runtime, (c) Phase 13 watch zones close with documented calibration, OR auto-lock July 15, 2026.
