The formal gated end-to-end verification *run* is not separately recorded; deployed-and-serving is what is asserted. **V9.29 amendment — MD/MO sub_position `why_this_level` why-higher-not-reached, internal symmetry with OR (NEW, June 3, 2026, SHIPPED + committed).** A one-line instruction added to `prompt-stage-md.js` (line 419) and `prompt-stage-mo.js` (line 521): the sub_position `why_this_level` field must now be "one sentence justification including why higher is not reached," matching `prompt-stage-or.js` line 671 (which already carried this). Brings all three scorers into symmetry on within-band ceiling-reasoning. **Scope of effect — INTERNAL-ONLY:** `why_this_level` lives in each scorer's `_internal.sub_position_predicates[]` block, which is stripped before Stage 2c (per V9.28 strip-before-Stage-2c pattern), never reaches the user-facing `.explanation`, and is not inspected by any gate. Scores, archetypes, sub_position arithmetic, lookups, and prose fields are all untouched — this changes only what the model commits in the internal reasoning trail. `node --check` clean; scoring blocks byte-identical; +1 line each. **Anchor predicates:** each scorer's sub_position `why_this_level` states both the level held and why the next-higher level is not reached; the field remains in `_internal`, not in `.explanation`. **Forbidden predicates:** `why_this_level` content surfacing in user-facing prose (still forbidden — V9.28 enum-leakage rule unchanged); any score/archetype/sub_position/lookup change (none — this is reasoning-trail enrichment only). **Why it matters:** this is the precondition for the V5.5 `direction`-surfacing design (below) — it makes MD/MO's internal within-band reasoning as complete as OR's before any surfacing build. **V9.29 is the FIFTEENTH V9.x amendment with concrete production deployment.** §9 V9 amendments tracking updated. **V9.28 Finding 2 — FLOOR sub-question RESOLVED, BAND-OVERLAP sub-question still OPEN.** V9.28 logged a single cross-metric observation as "open question pending explicit confirm or reconciliation": MD has floor 3.0 + overlapping bands; MO/OR have floor 1.0 + touching bands. That observation splits into two sub-questions, now disposed separately. **(a) FLOOR — LOCKED-as-intentional.** MD floor stays at 3.0. Basis (falsifiability asymmetry; per MasterReference P27 this is RECONSTRUCTION from the A1 archetype definition, not a recovered comparative-decision record): you cannot positively *evidence* zero demand from a described product — absence-of-demand-evidence is not evidence-of-demand-absence, so the honest low read is "speculative, no behavioral grounding" = A1 `speculative_need` = 3.0. MO and OR floor 1.0 because no-payment-capture and no-defensibility CAN be positively evidenced as absent; their 1-2 tail (MO `insufficient_evidence` / OR `no_defensibility_component`) is geometrically symmetric to the rare 7-8 top. Pushing MD to 1-2 was considered and rejected — you can't evidence total absence, and a truly dead idea already lands low through MO+OR's 1.0 floors in the composite, so MD doesn't need to go sub-3.0 to land the verdict low. The ChatGPT adversarial round held for this decision per Emre's discipline was completed (it converged). **(b) BAND-OVERLAP — still OPEN.** Whether MD's overlapping bands (a strong lower-archetype's upper sub-position can outscore a weak higher-archetype's lower sub-position — e.g. A2-upper 5.5 > A3-middle 5.4 > A3-lower 5.0) should be reconciled to MO/OR's clean touching-tier behavior (archetype rank strictly dominates) remains undecided; not blocking launch; revisit if it surfaces empirically. **V5.5 `direction`-surfacing design — DESIGNED-NOT-BUILT (forward note, explicitly NOT a V9.x amendment).** Recorded here so the next chat inherits it; it is NOT shipped behavior and therefore not an amendment to the contract. **Problem:** within-band reasoning already exists in every scorer's `_internal.sub_position_predicates[].why_this_level` (now uniform across MD/MO/OR per V9.29), but user-facing prose (MD/MO 3 fields, OR 4 fields) justifies the ARCHETYPE + binding constraint + direction-to-next-archetype, NOT why-this-position WITHIN the band. It is a surfacing gap, not a reasoning gap; not a granularity gap. **Locked design (build next chat):** fold within-band reasoning into the existing `direction` field — the natural host, it already answers "what would move higher" — as a TWO-CLAUSE field: (1) current-position clause translating lower/middle/upper via a plain-language band-position phrase ("lower/middle/upper part of this band"; never "sub-position", never internal enum names — TRANSLATE, don't transport, to respect the V9.28 enum-leakage forbid), (2) next-evidence clause. Skeleton-FAMILIES for openers (not an ordered illustrative list — that is the tcIncrementalNote/V9.22 whack-a-mole failure pattern; use the Stage 3 skeleton-family pattern that resisted it). Per-metric guards: OR `direction` must NOT re-explain its `binding_constraint_explanation` (separate field; §4 non-overlap risk specific to OR's four-field layout); MO `direction` must give evidence-threshold language only — no prescription / no "charge more" (preserves MO's prescription-free, profile-blind design). **Risks all logged:** enum-leakage, templating (this surface type is the historical templating hot-spot), Stage 2c synthesis overlap/drift (because `direction` feeds `.explanation` → Stage 2c). **Verification when built (MANDATORY, not optional):** end-to-end run (direction feeds Stage 2c), gate-suite re-run, cross-case templating check, length watch (two-clause structure vs the 1-2 sentence cap). **REJECTED alternatives (do not revisit without re-opening these explicitly):** post-lookup interpolation offset to spread scores ±0.1 (cosmetic, unjustifiable in prose, breaks `score = lookup[archetype][sub_position]` hardened in V5.3 G_ARITH_LOOKUP); more sub_position buckets 3→4-5 (DEFERRED until surfacing proves within-band reasoning is articulable — don't manufacture precision before proving existing precision is communicated). The May 18 "compression is design, not bug; most ideas SHOULD land at the cap" reframe is load-bearing and adjacent — any within-band discrimination change must consciously re-open it. **When the surfacing build ships, it becomes a V9.30 amendment** (real `direction` prose-contract change across all three scorers) and re-opens the full cascade. **V9 STILL OPEN.** Lock condition UNCHANGED from V9.28: V9 transitions OPEN → LOCKED when V5.0 production data confirms (a) score-shape guard never fires across first 100+ production evaluations, (b) scorer output schema stable at runtime, (c) Phase 13 watch zones close with documented calibration, OR auto-lock at July 15, 2026. V8-LOCKED preserved. **V9 amendments inventory:** 24 active total (the V9.28 inventory of 23 + V9.29 NEW; V9.24/V9.25/V9.26/V9.27 remain ABSORBED into V9.28; V9.9 and V9.11 retired). **Methodology reinforced (no new P-number):** read files before characterizing — two within-band overstatements this session (the "5.4 vs 6.0 within A4" error where 5.4 is A3-middle not within A4; the "OR is richest" claim where OR's only structural difference is the single why-higher-not-reached clause that V9.29 now mirrors into MD/MO) were caught by re-reading and corrected in-thread; prove changes byte-clean (`node --check` + diff showing only intended lines) before commit. **Closure cascade for this session (2 living docs):** (i) NarrativeContract V11.5 → V11.6 (this entry — V9.29 NEW + Finding 2 floor resolution + V5.5 surfacing forward-note); (ii) MasterReference V64 → V65 (deploy-state correction to LIVE + today's commits + V5.3 gates + V5.4 disposition + floor lock + V5.5 design-not-built + methodology). V4S32 *detected and corrected* the disease class; V5.0 *structurally prevents* it by replacing model-judgment scoring with mechanical lookup. The trajectory locked Principle P22 (V11.4): when three architectural moves all hit the same residual, the next move is a different mechanism class. V5.0 makes this concrete one level deeper — when *careful generation itself* is the residual, the next mechanism class is *remove the judgment*: replace model score-choice with a deterministic function of predicate commitments. The model still judges predicates with `evidence_cited` (where it's good — reading evidence shape from a packet); the system computes score (where the model rationalizes — anchor-fixing + co-decision per V11.3 P19). The Prosecutor Evolution (PE) feedback-loop conceptual scaffolding from V11.4 (PE1-PE5 sub-block) carries forward as user-feedback infrastructure concept but redesigned around mechanical-lookup observability (challenge-this-evaluation UX + predicate-commitment-level feedback + lookup-table-calibration cadence) when post-launch user signal warrants it. **V9.24 status (Stream A cap-rule prose-discipline):** ABSORBED into V9.28. The two-stream framing (Type 1 score-reader vs Type 2 prose-reader, both co-equal) remains operative as a UX principle; both audiences are still served — Type 1 reads the mechanical-lookup score (no longer subject to soft-engagement loophole because score is deterministic), Type 2 reads the synthesized prose. The cap-rule logic (MD/MO override-explicit, trigger-buyer-match, OR rule-precedence, MD-narrow-use + MO cap-landing precision, SCOPE clarifier) is now structurally encoded in scorer lookup tables, archetype entry criteria, binding-constraint subtype enums, and predicate-level enums. There is no model-generated score that could rationalize past a cap because there is no model-generated score at all. **V9 STILL OPEN.** Lock condition UPDATED: V9 transitions OPEN → LOCKED when V5.0 production data confirms (a) score-shape guard never fires across first 100+ production evaluations, (b) scorer output schema stable at runtime (all anchor predicates verified — score=lookup exactness, archetype enum, sub_position arithmetic, bucket mapping, enum-consistency across seam, `secondary_subtypes` object shape, schema_version `_v5`), (c) Phase 13 watch zones (OR fact-density pressure + high-band cases) close with documented calibration, OR auto-lock at July 15, 2026. V8-LOCKED preserved. **V9 amendments inventory:** 23 active total (3 pre-V4S29 conditional, of which V9.1 LANDED + V9.2 + V9.3 remain conditional + 5 V4S29-queued ABSORBED into V9.17 + V9.7 ABSORBED into V9.18 + V9.19 ABSORBED into V9.23 + 2 V4S29-queued still ACTIVE V9.12/V9.13 + V9.14 + V9.15 + V9.16 + V9.17 + V9.18 + V9.20 + V9.21 + V9.22 + V9.23 + V9.24 ABSORBED into V9.28 + V9.25 ABSORBED into V9.28 + V9.26 ABSORBED into V9.28 + V9.27 ABSORBED into V9.28 + V9.28 NEW; V9.9 and V9.11 retired). **3 new methodology principles proposed (P25-P27) for cascade lock in addition to P17-P20 (V11.3) and P21-P24 (V11.4) carried forward:** **P25 — Mechanical lookup beats careful generation when on a diminishing-returns curve at the judgment layer.** P22 (V11.4) established that when three architectural moves all hit the same residual, the answer is a different mechanism class. V5.0 makes this concrete one level deeper: when *careful generation itself* is the residual (V4S32 prosecutor caught the disease at ~10% even after V4S31 physical separation closed override frequency from 40% → 3%), the next mechanism class is *remove the judgment* — replace model score-choice with a deterministic function of predicate commitments. The model still judges predicates (where it's good); the system computes score (where the model rationalizes). The disease class moves from "model picks score then rationalizes prose" to structurally impossible. Pattern: when an adversarial-audit mechanism has working catch-rate (signal that the underlying decision is still wobbling, not noise), the next move is to mechanize the decision, not to make the audit smarter. Locked May 29, 2026. **P26 — Documentation voice vs operational voice STILL operative (recurring pattern, fifth structural session running).** Claude continues to draft documentation-voice (explaining intent, narrating reasoning, prose-balloon) when operational-voice (instructions only, named files, line counts, no narration) is the target preferred. Recurring methodology gap; should be treated as standing discipline at session entry rather than per-session correction. Locked-as-pattern May 29, 2026 (provisional — track whether self-correction frequency improves session-over-session). **P27 — Design history reconstruction discipline.** When asked "why did we design X like that" and the explicit comparative decision record cannot be located in project knowledge + past chats, name the semantic basis as RECONSTRUCTION from the design artifact's own content (e.g., archetype A1 `speculative_need`'s definition grounds MD floor 3.0), NEVER confabulate the comparative rationale ("we decided MD floor 3.0 vs MO/OR floor 1.0 *because* Y" when no record of that decision exists). Cite what is documented (the floor, the archetype semantic content, the structural choices) vs what is inferred (the comparative *why*). The MD-vs-MO/OR band asymmetry investigation this session was the canonical test — semantic basis present in A1 definitions + 7-vs-6 archetype packing consequence, comparative decision record not found, framing presented as reconstruction with explicit caveat.
