**Amendment V9.13 — Higher-order Prompt-Design Principle (NEW, V4S29 — methodology layer).** Cross-cutting design law amendment, not surface-specific. Validated by F2/F8a/F17/F18 quadruplet: any prompt change adding a single canonical "RIGHT" example creates a production template; multiple examples sharing syntactic shape produces the same disease. Distinctness over count is load-bearing. Principle text: *"No generation surface should rely on one canonical RIGHT example in its prompt. When examples are needed, include at least 3 structurally distinct examples, OR explicitly state that the examples are non-canonical. Distinct means different syntactic frame, not merely different domain nouns."* Pre-commit gate (3-point check from ChatGPT F18 round) enforces principle mechanically across all prompt-*.js files: ≥3 examples OR anti-copy / no two examples share primary syntactic frame / no example label implies "the one correct shape" without alternatives. **Split implementation per V4S29 dependency pressure-test:** Part 1 — pre-commit gate installation ships in Bundle 0 (Methodology infrastructure pre-Bundle-1) with WARN-on-existing/BLOCK-on-new semantics so all interim bundles benefit. Part 2 — V8 contract amendment (Principle text added as design law) ships in Bundle 6. Trigger: Bundle 0 (gate install) + Bundle 6 (contract amendment). Source: execution-plan-v5.1.md Higher-order Prompt-Design Principle lock + Bundle structure section.

**Amendment V9.14 — Methodology Principle 7: Counterfactual prompt tests precede architectural change (NEW, May 8, 2026, locked from F1 investigation, Bundle 2 closure).** Cross-cutting methodology amendment, parallel in scope to V9.13 (Higher-order Prompt-Design Principle). Principle text: *"Before committing to architectural restructuring (sidecar calls, stage splits, parallel pipelines, schema changes) as the cure for an observed instability, isolate the suspected mechanism via surgical prompt counterfactuals on the existing architecture. Architectural change is justified only when counterfactual evidence rules out simpler causes — sampler config, prompt structure, evidence weighting, output schema constraint."* **Scope:** applies to model-output behavior problems (variance, templating, framing instability, judgment drift). Does NOT apply to information-flow / validation / state-management problems — those legitimately require architectural reasoning first (a stage receiving forbidden context, a parser silently accepting invalid JSON, a route sending profile into profile-blind scoring). **Why it belongs in NarrativeContract:** Principle 7 governs how cure decisions are made for prompt-engineered narrative surfaces. NarrativeContract already governs cross-surface non-overlap and surface-level invariants. Principle 7 governs the meta-process of changing those invariants. It is the contract version of the methodology principle. **Productive tension acknowledged with V4S11 lesson** ("physical separation beats prompt rules"): both remain valid. Contract language at V9.14 lock should explicitly encode the productive tension and the test that distinguishes the two cases (counterfactual prompt tests reveal which lesson applies). **Operationalization artifact:** `runners/` directory shipped in Bundle 2 — `runStage2bWithOptions()` wrapper for custom prompt + custom sampler injection, pinned-anchor prompt counterfactual pattern, checkpoint/resume runner pattern, locked-decision-criteria-before-run pattern, full-pipeline verification harness pattern. Reusable for all future investigations. **Canonical case study reference:** `F1-investigation-case-study.md` (Bundle 2 closure artifact). **Status:** OPEN. Drafting work deferred per existing V9 lock condition policy; V9.14 contract language deferred to next ship that lands V9.x material (likely Bundle 4.1 with §3.4/§3.6 amendments). Trigger: future bundle that lands V9 amendments. Source: F1 investigation, Bundle 2 closure.

**Amendment V9.15 — Stage 2b internal scoring discipline + Structural Rigor Template Pattern (NEW, May 11, 2026, locked from V4S29 Stage 2b structural rigor template session ship).** Adds new internal-discipline subsection under existing §3.9-class Stage 2b interpretation surface, governing how MD/MO/OR scoring blocks operate within their existing surface-ownership contracts. Stage 2b's surface ownership (MD/MO/OR scores + Evidence Strength) is unchanged from §3.9 baseline. **Internal scoring discipline (locked):** (1) Top-line metric definitions open with embedded negations — each of MD, MO, OR names what the metric measures AND explicitly negates 3 common misreadings (e.g., MD: "Not whether the category exists, not whether the problem is real, not whether users would benefit"). (2) Pre-scoring questions per metric (existing block, unchanged). (3) Anti-inflation rules per metric — categorical rules forbidding common over-attribution patterns (existing block, unchanged this amendment). (4) Invalid bases enumeration with primary-anchor-vs-supporting-context qualifier — each metric (MD, MO) lists 5–6 bases that cannot serve as the *primary* anchor for that metric's score, while remaining acceptable as supporting context. OR receives parallel qualifier sentence appended to existing anti-inflation rules. (5) Metric-local uncertainty rule — when packet evidence plausibly supports two adjacent score bands, score defaults to LOWER band unless packet contains specific high-trust anchor justifying higher. Each of MD, MO, OR has its own metric-local uncertainty rule placed INSIDE that metric's block; NO universal "applies to MD/MO/OR" framing (universal framing would recreate the holistic-impression problem §3.9 quarantine architecture exists to prevent). (6) Binding cap at 7.0+ for MD and MO — each metric's cap requires named buyer + named anchor evidence to permit scoring at 7.0 or higher. MO cap includes embedded **hedge discipline**: uncertainty attacking metric core ("requires critical mass," "depends on cold-start," "unit economics uncertain") without counter-anchor caps MO at 7.0 regardless of other positive signals. OR cap remains at 6.0+ (untouched in this session; defer to future calibration). (7) Required explanation structure with (a)/(b)/exit triage — each metric explanation must include rubric-level justification grounded in packet evidence AND a proof point or validation move: path (a) cite concrete evidence in packet, path (b) identify realistic test, honest exit if neither possible ("No realistic [proof / validation] path is identifiable from this evidence"). Anti-generic guardrail: forbidden generic suggestions enumerated per metric. (8) Cross-metric independence verification — after all three metric scores and explanations are drafted, but before finalizing output, run three sequential independence verifications: MD–MO, MD–OR, MO–OR. Each verification fires at ≥6.5 threshold on both metrics, checks that each cites different causal facts (buyer existence is primarily MD, payment context is primarily MO, replication barrier is primarily OR), and instructs lower-the-weaker-metric remediation if two metrics rely on same underlying signal. **MUST NOT drift into:** universal cross-metric scoring rules (preserve metric-local placement), Stage 2c synthesis content (Row 6 path (b) validation moves are metric-internal scoring justifications NOT roadmap suggestions), TC scoring (separate isolated call), profile-aware reasoning (Stage 2b is profile-blind per §3.9 quarantine). **Anchor predicates:** explicit rubric-level mention at start of every explanation ("Score X.X, rubric level Y–Z"); specific buyer + specific anchor naming in validation moves; explicit hedge-discipline acknowledgment when cap fires; anti-inflation rule citation visible in reasoning. **Forbidden predicates:** "category is large" / "competitors exist" / "TAM is X" as primary MD anchors above 6.0; "subscription model exists" / "success fee aligns incentives" as primary MO anchors above 6.0; "workflow is differentiated" / "vertical positioning" as primary OR anchors above 6.0; generic validation suggestions without named entities. **Verification anchors for B10b:** 7.0+ disease rate on F7 audit-labeled Generous cases hard threshold zero (observed 0 of 15 in V4S29 verification); watch zones documented (6.0–6.5 generosity zone where Rows 4/6/8 fire but don't always pull score all the way down); honest exit clause firing rate 0 of 105 in sample, status pending deliberately-thin-evidence stress test; path (a)/(b) distribution observed 19%/57% with (b) default tendency; single-run interpretation spikes ≤1 of 5 reruns per case on any metric (V4S29 observed 1/5 spikes on A3 MD 7.5 and MAT2-senior OR 7.0, below disease threshold); cross-metric independence (Row 9) passing in V4S29 sample with no observed case where two metrics ≥6.5 cited same underlying signal. **Empirical state at amendment lock (May 11, 2026):** 8 canonical F7 audit cases × 5 reruns = 40 PRO pipeline runs / fixture mode on / HTTP-based against local dev server. 5 of 7 assessable cases pass per-case verification criteria (L1 N/A — gates upstream). 2 hard failures: A3 (MD 7.5 spike, 1 of 5 runs), MAT2-senior (OR 7.0 spike, 1 of 5 runs) — interpretation stochasticity, not systematic disease. 2 watch zones: MAT3-tna and MAT2-beginner land at 6.5 not 6.0 on 60–80% of runs. B2 (Mixed CONTROL) and M2 (Well-justified CONTROL) false-positive guards both pass. Prose quality outcomes (105 explanations analyzed): 100% rubric-level grounding, 40% specific-number citation, 19% path-(a) / 57% path-(b) / 0% honest-exit. **Status:** SHIPPED partial cure. Disease pattern (60%+ rate of 7.0+ events on Generous cases at May 10 baseline) is cured. Residual 1-in-5 interpretation stochasticity remains, scoped to model-judgment layer where prompt changes have diminishing returns. ChatGPT framing accepted: "successful structural upgrade, partial scoring cure, not final calibration closure." **Cross-cutting addition to §3.13 — Structural Rigor Template Pattern methodology layer:** multi-row × multi-metric structural rigor templates can be applied to scoring stages to standardize internal discipline across metrics. Pattern requires: (1) symmetry of discipline NOT placement (universal "applies to all metrics" framing recreates holistic-impression problem); (2) cap + band discipline + structure operate as system not redundant defenses; (3) primary-anchor-vs-supporting-context qualifier on invalid bases prevents both inflation and false-positive suppression; (4) (a)/(b)/exit triage for required explanation structure (empirical observation: model defaults to (b); honest exit rarely fires; (a) under-fires when concrete evidence exists; triage discipline incomplete, refinement deferred); (5) cross-metric independence verification placed AFTER drafting, three sequential pair-checks at ≥6.5 threshold; (6) verification criteria locked before runs (Methodology Principle 6 reaffirmed) — pattern can intentionally produce "technical FAIL with substantive partial cure" outcome which is the honest readout when criteria assume more determinism than system delivers; (7) pattern is portable to other scoring stages (Stage 2a packet construction, Stage 2c synthesis, Stage 1 evidence aggregation, Stage 3 roadmap) — each session ports row pattern but adapts content to surface's own logic. Pattern locked methodology-layer principle, parallel scope to V9.13 + V9.14. Trigger: SHIPPED May 11, 2026 (V4S29 Stage 2b session) — V9.15 is the first V9.x amendment with concrete production deployment; contract language drafted at amendment time per cascade (not deferred). Source: V4S29_Stage2b_Closure.md (session record), execution-plan-v5.4 amendment. **Connected amendments:** Pattern portable to upcoming Stage 2a structural session (V9.16 candidate — SHIPPED May 12, 2026), Stage 2c structural session, Stage 1 structural session, Stage 3 structural session.

**Amendment V9.16 — Stage 2a internal packet-construction discipline (NEW, May 12, 2026, locked from V4S29 Stage 2a structural rigor template session ship).** Adds new internal-discipline subsection under existing §3.10 Stage 2a Packet Sparse-Input Discipline interpretation surface, governing how MD/MO/OR evidence packets are constructed within their existing surface-ownership contracts. Stage 2a's surface ownership (3 packets MD/MO/OR with admissible_facts / strongest_positive / strongest_negative / unresolved_uncertainty per packet, architectural quarantine layer per V4S9 lock) is unchanged from §3.10 baseline. The existing §3.10 contract covers Stage 2a packet shape *under sparse-input trigger*; V9.16 extends the discipline to non-sparse packet construction with parallel structure to V9.15 (Stage 2b internal scoring discipline). **Internal packet-construction discipline (locked):** (1) **Packet definition with embedded negations per packet** — MD packet defines "capturable demand surviving friction" + 3 explicit negations (not whether the category exists / not whether the problem is real / not whether users would benefit). MO packet defines "durable revenue from specific buyer or payer at specific price despite substitute or payment friction" + 3 explicit negations (not theoretical market size / not generic buyer-domain wealth / not solution-to-pain inference). OR packet defines "credible structural wedge incumbents cannot easily replicate" + 3 explicit negations (not feature novelty / not architectural choice / not category-shift narrative). Embedded negations carry the "what this packet does NOT measure" discipline into Stage 2a packet construction, preventing facts that map to negated patterns from anchoring strongest_positive. (2) **Admissibility dimensions anchored to Row 1** — each packet has 4–5 admissibility dimensions stating which fact patterns satisfy the packet's definition. MO packet preserves verbatim the MO PACKET SPARSE-INPUT RULE from V4S28 B5 (character-for-character locked contract clause). OR packet adds the feature-gap qualifier: feature-gap facts admissible only when paired with replication-difficulty evidence. (3) **Categorical exclusions + primary-anchor-vs-supporting-context qualifier with primary-framing paraphrase test** — each packet enumerates 3 fact patterns whose primary framing matches the packet's negation patterns. Such facts may appear as supporting context in admissible_facts BUT cannot anchor strongest_positive. Primary-framing paraphrase test: *if a fact can be restated as one of the packet's Row 1 negations without materially changing meaning, it may appear as supporting context but cannot anchor strongest_positive*. Plus OR competitor-gap safeguard (feature gap alone insufficient as OR anchor; must be paired with replication-difficulty evidence) and no-qualified-anchor outcome (option b — if no admissible fact passes primary-framing test as anchor, strongest_positive is omitted or marked as "no qualified anchor identified" rather than forced). (4) **5-priority source-tag selection sequence (pipeline-wide)** — fixed priority hierarchy for selecting which fact to use when multiple source tags compete: `[competitor: Name]` → `[domain_flag: ...]` → `[idea_description]` (RESERVED for facts ABOUT the proposed idea itself, NOT competitor-derived facts the user happens to mention) → `[narrative_field]` → `[user_claim]`. The `[idea_description]` tiebreaker is the most-corrected position: it serves the user's own product description, not facts the user happens to repeat from competitor research. Maintains 5-tag space closed per V4S20 + B5 + B6 architectural lock. (5) **Anchor selection sequence (deterministic)** — when multiple facts pass admissibility for a packet, anchor selection follows: direct-relevance to packet definition → trust-tier (source-tag priority) → specificity (named entities, named numbers, named friction events) → first-listed tiebreaker. Plus MO substantive tiebreaker (pick fact that most directly attacks buyer-pays-this-price claim under MO ties, NOT structural-default "always pick competitor-side") and OR LLM-substitution exception (if domain_flag = llm_substitution_risk is present, that fact overrides competitor-side tiebreaker for OR). Both tiebreaker rules use substantive discrimination per Methodology Principle 10 (not structural defaults). (6) **Three-lens uncertainty discipline (MARKET-SIDE / INPUT-SIDE / EVIDENCE-SIDE)** — unresolved_uncertainty must select one of three lenses based on substantive question, not structural default. MARKET-SIDE (default for non-sparse): names a specific buyer or market dynamic the evaluation cannot resolve from available evidence. INPUT-SIDE: used only when resolving a missing input would directly resolve the unknown (not as blame-mode for sparse inputs). EVIDENCE-SIDE: used rarely, only when uncertainty is about quality of evidence base itself (search retrieval, competitor coverage). Anti-generic guardrail: forbidden generic uncertainty framings ("more research needed" / "would need to validate" / "depends on execution") without naming a specific verifiable question. Lens selection per Methodology Principle 10 — substantive discrimination, not structural default. (7) **Fact-density operational discipline** — 3–4 facts per packet default; hard cap 4 facts (V9.16 NEW); sparse-input target 2 facts (preserved from V9 §3.10); fourth-fact rule (4th fact must add substantively distinct evidence dimension, not echo prior 3); anti-padding test (if any of 4 facts can be removed without changing the packet's evidence picture, packet should have 3 not 4). (8) **11-item cross-packet verification with new Items 7 and 11** — extended cross-packet check at end of Stage 2a output. Item 7 NEW: primary-framing paraphrase test — for each packet's strongest_positive, restate the fact as Row 1 negation language and verify it does NOT materially preserve the original claim; if it does, demote to supporting context. Item 11 NEW: anchor diversity check — no single competitor or fact may anchor strongest_positive across all 3 packets (anchor monoculture). Preserves existing items 1–6 and 8–9 from V9 §3.10. **MUST NOT drift into:** profile-aware reasoning (Stage 2a remains profile-blind per V4S9 + B6 atomic three-strip), score implications (Stage 2a is sorter not analyst — produces thin or thick packets, not low or high scores), Stage 2b scoring rules (Row 4 / 6 / 8 fact selection priorities are packet-construction discipline NOT scoring rules; Stage 2b's scoring discipline is V9.15 territory), Stage 2c synthesis (cross-packet verification Items 7/11 are admissibility checks NOT narrative coherence checks), MO PACKET SPARSE-INPUT RULE alteration (V4S28 B5 contract clause preserved character-for-character; V9.16 ADDS discipline layers but does NOT rewrite locked sparse-input clauses). **Anchor predicates:** explicit packet-definition statement at top of each packet output (when serialized in admissible_facts metadata or implicit through fact selection); source-tag attribution visible on every admissible fact per locked 5-tag space; specific buyer / specific anchor / specific friction-event naming in strongest_positive; three-lens unresolved_uncertainty framing with named verifiable question; 3-4 fact density per packet on non-sparse inputs; primary-framing-test compliance visible through absence of negation-paraphrasable facts as anchors. **Forbidden predicates:** facts with `[user_claim]` source tag anchoring strongest_positive on MD or MO packets (preserves V4S20 + B5 lock); generic uncertainty framings without named verifiable questions; competitor monoculture in strongest_positive across packets; 5+ facts per packet on any input (hard cap); facts that paraphrase to Row 1 negations anchoring strongest_positive; INPUT-SIDE uncertainty lens applied to inputs where input gap would NOT resolve the unknown (input-blame monoculture per Methodology Principle 10). **Verification anchors for B10b:** primary-framing violations across all anchors hard threshold zero (V4S29 Stage 2a verification: 0 violations across 105 anchors); density hard-cap violations zero (V4S29: 0 violations, 0 packets at 5 facts vs pre-session 77 packets at 5); lens consistency 100% MARKET-SIDE on non-sparse inputs (V4S29: 105/105 packets MARKET-SIDE — lens-flipping disease eliminated); anchor monoculture instances zero (V4S29: 0 instances per Item 11 detector); tag determinism observed at higher variance than design intent (V4S29: A3 OR regulatory facts 4 distinct tags across 11 observations — no score harm since A3 OR flat at 4.5 across all 5 reruns, but flagged as Item 4 calibration target); anchor stability fingerprint-test interpretation caveat (60-char fingerprints conflate conceptual stability with paraphrase variance; read Layer 1 fingerprint results alongside actual packet contents). **Empirical state at amendment lock (May 12, 2026):** 8 canonical F7 audit cases × 5 reruns = 40 PRO pipeline runs through `runners/run-v4s29-stage2a-rigor-verification-http.js` / fixture mode on / HTTP-based against local dev server. **Layer 1 (Stage 2a behavioral, 105 packets analyzed):** lens consistency 100% MARKET-SIDE (105/105) ✅; density hard-cap 0 violations ✅; density 5-fact elimination 0 packets at 5 (pre-session: 77) ✅; primary-framing 0 violations (105/105 anchors) ✅; anchor monoculture 0 instances ✅; anchor stability 3-5 distinct fingerprints/5 ⚠️ HIGH (paraphrase-intolerant test artifact, not disease); tag determinism on A3 OR 4 distinct tags ❌ DRIFT (no score harm). **Layer 2 (score stability, 40 runs):** 5 of 7 assessable cases pass per locked criteria (L1 N/A — gates upstream); 1 hard failure A3 (MD 7.5 spike, 1 of 5 runs — paraphrase-emphasis variance disease class, Stage 2b territory); 1 false-positive guard failure M2 (OR band drift 4.5 → 5.0–6.5 — Stage 2a now extracts legitimate OR evidence baseline missed, NOT downgrade direction); 1 watch zone MAT2-beginner MO ceiling at 6.5 not 6.0. **Three watch-zone spikes from V9.15 session ELIMINATED:** MAT2-senior OR 7.0 (Row 5 anchor stability), MAT2-beginner MO 7.0 (Row 1 negations + Row 3 primary-framing + Row 8 Item 7 defense-in-depth pathway), MAT3-tna MO 7.0 (defense-in-depth pathway operative). **Qualitative downstream Stage 2b explanation quality transformed** despite Stage 2b prompt unchanged this session — evidence → counter-evidence → uncertainty → concrete-next-step pattern across all 7 assessable cases with decision-grade recommendations (numbers + durations + metrics + decision criteria; cross-case structural consistency enables multi-idea hub comparability). **Status:** SHIPPED partial cure with documented residuals per ChatGPT framing accepted: "shipped with residuals — criteria correctly flagged residual risk but were too narrow to capture broader product-quality improvement." Disease class transformation: pre-Stage-2a-session disease class was anchor-selection variance (Stage 2a picks different facts across reruns); post-Stage-2a-session disease class is **paraphrase-emphasis variance** (Stage 2a picks defensible fact deterministically but paraphrases with varying emphasis; Stage 2b reads emphasis as score-relevant). New variance class, lower amplitude, Stage 2b interpretation territory — deferred to future Stage 2b calibration session. **Cross-cutting addition to §3.13 — Structural Rigor Template Pattern methodology layer extension (V9.15 lineage):** V9.15 locked the pattern's portability to scoring stages. V9.16 demonstrates the pattern is portable to upstream architectural-quarantine stages (Stage 2a packet construction) with the following adaptations: (i) "metric" replaced by "packet" as the unit of row application (3 packets × 8 rows instead of 4 metrics × 9 rows); (ii) scoring rules (Stage 2b Row 4 invalid bases / Row 5 caps / Row 9 cross-metric independence) replaced by packet-construction rules (Stage 2a Row 4 tag-priority / Row 5 anchor selection / Row 8 cross-packet verification); (iii) "uncertainty defaults to lower band" (Stage 2b Row 8) replaced by "uncertainty lens selected by substantive question, not structural default" (Stage 2a Row 6 — Methodology Principle 10 enforcement); (iv) verification surface bifurcates into Layer 1 (behavioral, upstream stage's own territory) and Layer 2 (score stability, downstream effect) — Methodology Principle 11 (Stage upstream of scoring affects scoring through downstream interpretation, not direct intervention) — frontier of variance moves rather than eliminates when applying rigor template to upstream stage; (v) "shipped with residuals" closure framing applies same as V9.15 — technical criterion result and product-quality result evaluated separately. Pattern locked methodology-layer principle, parallel scope to V9.13 + V9.14 + V9.15. **Amendment V9.17 — Stage 2c internal synthesis discipline + Schema Preservation (Option C) + Per-user multi-idea pattern recognition watch zone (NEW, May 13, 2026, locked from V4S29 Stage 2c structural reorganization session ship).** Adds new internal-discipline subsection under existing §3.2 Summary text + §3.3 Risk 1 (market_category) + §3.4 Risk 3 (founder_fit) + §3.5 Risk 2 (trust_adoption) interpretation surfaces, governing how synthesis output is structured across the 4 user-facing slots. Stage 2c's surface ownership (Summary + failure_risks array with 3 slots + archetype enum) is unchanged from §3.2-§3.5 baseline; the existing contracts cover slot territory and unique-question boundaries. V9.17 extends the discipline to internal synthesis structure with adapted parallel structure to V9.15 (Stage 2b internal scoring discipline) and V9.16 (Stage 2a internal packet-construction discipline). **Adaptation pattern for synthesis stage:** "metric" (V9.15) and "packet" (V9.16) replaced by "cognitive job" — Stage 2c has TWO fundamentally different cognitive jobs (Job 1 Summary synthesizes the verdict; Job 2 failure_risks differentiates failure modes by threat agent: market / users / founder) requiring asymmetric per-job templates plus cross-cutting coherence rows. The 9-row × 4-metric symmetric template (V9.15) and 8-row × 3-packet symmetric template (V9.16) are replaced by a 5-block × multi-row architecture. **Internal synthesis discipline (locked):** **Block A — Summary synthesis discipline (10 rows, 30 examples):** A1 synthesis-not-enumeration (Summary must integrate threat categories without listing them); A2 case-truth integration (Summary references upstream MD/MO/OR/TC/EvStr scores AND Stage 1 competition AND Stage 2a packets as integrated evidence); A3 opener archetype rotation (α profile-led when founder IS case-truth / β tension-led when cross-metric tension is binding / γ market-led when category structure is binding / δ decisive-uncertainty-led when unresolved variable is binding / ε profile-gap-led when founder-fit IS the binding constraint); A4 band-driven content selection (low-band leads with binding weakness per HARD RULE preserved from V4S28 B3; mid-band leads with structural tension per MIXED-BAND FRAMING RULE preserved from V4S28 B3.5; high-band leads with what's working per TONE CALIBRATION); A5 verbatim profile attribution (P1-S1 stem-match rule — any "Your X years as [role]" reference must verbatim-match profile.education); A6 specificity test on closing sentence (closing must name specific buyer segment OR specific uncertainty OR specific behavior OR specific price point OR specific channel OR specific evidence gap); A7 cross-metric tension naming (when tension shape changes case read, name structurally — not gated by 2.0 spread threshold); A8 score-band tone alignment; A9 forbidden inferences from profile (no employer-domain / capability-level / role-type / intensifier / seniority inference beyond profile.education verbatim); A10 sentence advancement (every sentence advances synthesis — no restatement; 4-category classification New/Integration/Sharpening/Bloat with Bloat forbidden). **Block B — Risk 1 + Risk 2 differentiation discipline (7 rows, 11 examples):** B1 threat-agent anchoring (Risk 1 = market structure / Risk 2 = users / Risk 3 = founder; non-overlap enforced); B2 mechanism specification (each Risk names the operating mechanism by which the threat materializes, not just the threat category); B3 specificity test (Risk must name specific competitors, specific user-segment, specific friction mechanism); B4 Risk 1 frame differentiation (5 frames: Frame 1 relational moat / Frame 2 category consolidation / Frame 3 substitution from different category / Frame 4 category-shape regulatory / Frame 5 fragmentation — per-case Frame selection driven by case-truth, no default frame); B5 plan-changing test (a threat the user already plans around isn't a Risk; a threat that would change go/no-go or first-move IS); B6 slot-territory enforcement (no cross-territory drift); B7 anti-template structural diversity (cross-case structural distinctness on Risk 1 + Risk 2 openings). **Block C — Risk 3 firing + archetype discipline (9 rows, 24 examples):** C1 substantive-fire test (Risk 3 fires when knowing founder identity changes the case's read in a way that changes go/no-go or first move; doesn't fire for ornamental founder gaps); C2 tri-bucket classification (INSIDER multi-year practitioner role IN target domain / PARTIAL-INSIDER adjacent operational role OR role-related but not buyer-side decision-maker / OUTSIDER no operational role in target domain); C3 Decision Procedure (7-step flow: Step 1 case-truth extraction → Step 2 tri-bucket classification → Step 3 substantive-fire test → Step 4 archetype selection per binding gap → Step 5 INTERNAL subtype disambiguation A1/A2/A3 → Step 6 sentence-1 subject discipline → Step 7 closing-direction); C4 archetype A internal subtype split (A1 engineering capacity gap / A2 AI-data system capability gap / A3 integration-compliance-security infrastructure gap; **Schema Preservation Option C: A1/A2/A3 are INTERNAL REASONING SUBTYPES only — JSON output emits "A" for all three subtypes; downstream Stage 3 prompt unchanged; old test runners b10a-gates.js + run-archetypes.js continue to work without modification; historical B10a baseline comparisons remain clean**); C5 sentence-1 subject discipline (mismatch-as-subject not build-difficulty-as-subject — Risk 3 frames founder-task mismatch; per-archetype banned patterns enforced; predicate-balance discipline); C6 founder-task mismatch anchor (Risk 3's content is the gap between founder's demonstrated profile attributes on the binding dimension AND the task's specific execution requirements on that dimension); C7 archetype-evidence-driven content selection (per-archetype evidence anchors: A subtypes anchor on engineering/AI-data/regulated-infrastructure specifics; B anchors on buyer-network specifics; C anchors on credentialed-buyer trust specifics; pending Free Pipeline Integrity Review session). **Block D-prompt — Cross-output coherence (3 rows):** D1 same evidence base across surfaces (Summary + Risks consume same packets + Stage 1 + scores, no invention on either); E2 within-archetype variance discipline (per-archetype Risk 3 openings vary across cases sharing that archetype — current cure incomplete, elevated watch zone). **MUST NOT drift into:** Stage 3 territory (Main Bottleneck classification, roadmap phases — Stage 3 owns these per §3.6/§3.7); Within-case-rerun stability is invisible to single-read users (per Methodology Principle 12), but per-user-multi-idea exposure surfaces it. (iii) Reference-don't-restate cross-block discipline — coherence rows REFERENCE the rows they govern, do NOT RESTATE content (X-2 initially restated E-2 calibration matrix, ChatGPT caught duplication; same architectural pattern as MB-7 referencing MB-8, E-5 referencing MB-8); (iv) Discipline framing not verification framing in runtime prompts — Block X is generation-time discipline, verification harness is operational infrastructure; (v) Non-contradiction over strict alignment for cross-stage coherence — MB and Summary can be coherent without saying the same thing; the compatibility test replaces abstract "operates within case-truth" framing; (vi) Materiality discipline closes "at least one risk" loophole — without materiality, MB could connect to marginal Risk 3 while ignoring dominant risks; with materiality, MB must connect to the dominant risk cluster; (vii) Architectural pivot mid-session is legitimate when original scope reveals posture mismatch — Block T (Tools) and Block R (Roadmap) weren't bad designs but wrong cognitive job for Stage 3's diagnostic posture; these belong in verification documentation, not generation prompt; same category violation pattern caught earlier in MB-8 (corpus distribution percentages) and E-5 (per-corpus calibration). Remove `phases` / `tools` array expectations from `analyze-pro/route.js`, save logic, schema, and rendering. Move TC visual from Screen 1 to Screen 2 (relocate alongside MB + Estimates). Remove Roadmap and Tools sections from EvaluationView. Update ComparisonView, save/branch/re-evaluate routes. Per locked execution order: no Execution Plan feature build at this point — that comes after Stage 1 + Stage TC sessions and a dedicated planning session; (b) **Stage 3 testing** — performed during/after cleanup pass. Test runner validates MB classification stability across reruns (31% flip cure), MB enum distribution (Capital/runway fires on D-archetype, NULL Trust default cure holds), MB explanation prose variance (77% verbatim cure), Estimates duration/difficulty calibration, commitment beat discipline, cross-stage coherence with Stage 2c; (c) **Stage 1 structural session** — promoted to NEXT after cleanup; (d) **Stage TC structural session** — after Stage 1; (e) **Execution Plan feature planning session** — after Stage 1 + Stage TC, discusses everything decided in Stage 3 session (three-screen flow, Execution Plan feature design, TC relocation, credit-only business model) to form an execution plan for the Execution Plan feature build; (f) **Execution Plan feature build** — after planning session; (g) AI-builder vs general-builder audience calibration — deferred future session; (h) Difficulty axis review (Solo Founder Feasibility vs current 4-value enum) — deferred future session; (i) UX bridge spec — deterministic UI copy at end of Screen 2 ("Ready to turn this diagnosis into an execution plan?") — flagged for Execution Plan feature build session. **Methodology lessons locked from this session (8 lessons):** (1) Architectural pivot mid-session is legitimate when original scope reveals posture mismatch — Block T and Block R weren't bad designs, they were good designs for the wrong cognitive job; Stage 3's diagnostic posture and Tools/Roadmap's supportive posture conflict at the user's commitment stage; the pivot resolved the conflict by separating posture into separate screens. (2) Reference don't restate (cross-block discipline) — coherence rows REFERENCE the rows they govern, they don't RESTATE the content; X-2 initially restated E-2's per-MB calibration matrix, ChatGPT caught the duplication; same architectural pattern as MB-7 referencing MB-8, E-5 referencing MB-8. (3) MB stability over Estimates drift — failure protocols across X-2/X-3/X-4 all preserve MB selection by default when case data supports it; Estimates is the more frequently-failing surface, MB is the upstream anchor; internal consistency with E-1 MB-derivation principle. (4) Discipline framing not verification framing in runtime prompts — Block X is generation-time discipline; the verification harness is operational infrastructure; "verification" language in a prompt risks model treating Block X as a runtime audit step instead of generation discipline. (5) Non-contradiction over strict alignment for cross-stage coherence — MB and Summary can be coherent without saying the same thing; the compatibility test (explains / narrows / gates / compounds) replaces the abstract "operates within case-truth" framing. (6) Materiality discipline closes the "at least one risk" loophole — without materiality, MB could connect to a marginal Risk 3 founder-fit gap while ignoring dominant market/competition risks; with materiality, MB must connect to the dominant risk cluster. (7) Documentation must match reality — when Tools and Roadmap moved out of Stage 3, the prompt's file header and Block X-5 cross-row interface text both had to update; Stage 3 docs don't reference what Stage 3 no longer does. (8) Pre-emptive verification specifications create category violations — X-5 initially included a 4-step sampling procedure, 10% overlap threshold, and harness routing references; these belong in verification documentation, not generation prompt; same category violation pattern caught earlier in MB-8 and E-5.

**Amendments V9.19 → V9.29 — recorded in the header version-log + §8, not re-expanded here (append-only note, June 4, 2026).** The detailed "Amendment V9.x —" bodies in this §9 list run V9.1 → V9.18 (the V4S29 structural-session arc). The amendments that landed afterward — V9.19 (Stage 2c C7 archetype-selection patch, May 16), V9.20 (Stage TC structural rewrite + V9.1 LANDED, May 17), V9.21/V9.22/V9.23 (Stage 2c Summary / Stage TC / Stage 2c C7 anti-template + structural patches, May 18-19), V9.24 (Stage 2b Stream-A score discipline, May 19), V9.25/V9.26/V9.27 (V4S30 schema externalization / V4S31 two-call separation / V4S32 Prosecutor+Repair, May 19-21), V9.28 (V5.0 Mechanical-Lookup Scoring Discipline, May 29 — V9.24/V9.25/V9.26/V9.27 ABSORBED), and V9.29 (MD/MO `why_this_level` why-higher-not-reached internal symmetry, June 3) — are each fully documented in the dated **"Updated:" header version-log at the top of this document** and in the §8 record, per the append-only convention. They were not back-filled as separate detailed bodies in this list; the header log is their authoritative detailed record. This note exists so the V9.18 → V9.30 jump in this list is not read as a gap.

**Amendment V9.30 — MO code-side DISPLAY score + 12b explicit `_internal.override_applied` trace (NEW, June 4, 2026, SHIPPED to production; Arc 7).** The FIRST V9.x amendment that moves a scoring computation into code — the V11.6/V11.7 "becomes a V9.30 amendment AT SHIP TIME" forecast, realized — but **narrower than forecast: DISPLAY-only, so V9.28 is UNMODIFIED.** `.score` remains the model-emitted `lookup[archetype][sub_position]`; the code value is a separate, decoupled `display_score`. **What shipped (`src/lib/services/scoring.js` + `src/app/api/analyze-pro/route.js`, committed + pushed by Emre):** (a) `computeMoDisplayScore` / `computeMoScoreDiagnostic` compute a finer MO score from the committed `_internal.sub_position_predicates` (recompute sum-from-components — cures `G_ARITH_SUM` for the display value — apply the two prompt overrides, interpolate within band); `route.js` sets `ev.monetization.display_score` at FINAL assembly (after overall_score / Stage 2c / Stage 3, after the `_internal` restore); frontend renders `display_score ?? score`; a CONSISTENCY GUARD falls back to coarse `.score` when code's recomputed bucket disagrees with the model's declared `sub_position`. (b) 12b — `computeMoOverrideTrace` is the single source for MO's two bucket overrides (PRIORITY_PULL + the arithmetically-unreachable GLOBAL_SP_CAP), consumed by both the display score and the trace so they cannot drift; `route.js` writes explicit `_internal.override_applied {rule, arithmetic_bucket, final_bucket, trigger}` (or `null`) at assembly, computed from SP values only — it never reads or rewrites the declared `sub_position` (no silent relabeling); downstream reads `effective_bucket = override_applied?.final_bucket ?? sub_position`. **Decoupling is the risk-free shape:** `.score` and ALL downstream behavior are provably unchanged — source-read confirmed `calculateOverallScore`, Stage 2c band gates (key off `overall_score` 5.0/6.5), and Stage 3 (`MD/MO < 5.0` modifier) all read `.score`; the fine value is out of every feedback loop. **Full code-CANONICAL migration (code owns `.score`) → investigated → RED, not pursued:** (1) ~27% non-rule-shaped model-vs-SP-sum bucket disagreement (the binding-constraint pull beyond strict PRIORITY_PULL is the anti-inflation moat; code-canonical would override it by fiat and inflate exactly those cases); (2) MO run-to-run variance is dominated by upstream Stage 2a packet divergence (rfull: 13/15 reruns moved the bucket, packet varied 15/15) which code cannot touch. The movement is the accepted explain-the-difference evidence-tracking, not scorer noise. **MD + OR code-side display → DECLINED:** the MO trick delivers only where the compressed cluster's `sub_position_sum` VARIES; MD's A4 wall is 18×sum=2 (interpolation inert → resolution multi-dimensional → PROSE) and OR's dominant cluster is 16×sum=−1 honest-equivalence (spreading manufactures false distinction). Mechanism self-protects (constant-sum → one value → cannot fake precision). **Bounded doctrine LOCKED: code is the DISPLAY authority, not the SCORE authority** — bucket placement carries judgment the arithmetic doesn't capture, so V9.28's mechanical-lookup `.score` stays canonical. **Anchor predicates:** MO `display_score` computed in code at final assembly, NEVER overwrites `.score`; frontend renders `display_score ?? score`; consistency guard falls back to coarse on bucket disagreement; `_internal.override_applied` is the single explicit record of a fired override, computed from committed SP values, `sub_position` left exactly as the model emitted it; `computeMoOverrideTrace` is the single source of the override rules. **Forbidden predicates:** code overwriting the canonical `.score`; silently relabeling `sub_position` to reconcile an override; a `display_score` that contradicts the committed bucket / prose (guard prevents it); applying the MO display trick to MD or OR (constant-sum clusters — inert or dishonest). **Empirics (clean june328 baseline, 26 MO):** fallback 38.5% (all guard_mismatch), max delta 0.6, crosses_5 = 0, distinct 9→13 (+4); GLOBAL_SP_CAP arithmetically unreachable (spA≤1 ⟹ max sum 4 = middle) so PRIORITY_PULL is the only live override (fired 0× across the 26+49-case runs); 17/17 display regression + 8/8 trace tests. **Related:** 12a (V5.8 — MD always emit `_internal`) PARKED (real fix is fragile model-emission; code can only guarantee structural presence + honest degradation; pays off only with the deferred explain-feature; the MD-specific ~4% miss-rate root cause is banked for that session). The V5.5 `direction`-prose-surfacing build remains DESIGNED-NOT-BUILT and would be a separate later amendment. **V9.30 is the SIXTEENTH V9.x amendment with concrete production deployment; V9.28 remains the authoritative scoring discipline, UNMODIFIED. Total V9 amendments tracked: 25 active.** **Status:** SHIPPED to production (`bf09382` + the display/12b commits). Source: Arc 7 session record (this session's transcript + run artifacts); cascade — MasterReference V67 + ActionQueue V10.
